jātau jātau sadā dṛṣṭāḥ saugataistattvadarśibhiḥ // 7.129 //
||aneka sukhasaṃsāraḥ viṣayātmaka eva
anekasukhasaṃsāro viṣayeṣu hi vidyate /
viṣayaiśca bhavet sarva jātau jātau prajāyate // 7.130 //
kaṣṭairyairanakāmairna śakyate 'mūḍhacetasā /
punastāneva mohāndhāḥ sevante 'kṛtabuddhayaḥ // 7.131 //
||viṣayaśatrusevinaḥ bāliśāḥ bhavanti
varjate hi sadā śatruvañcanāśaṅkayā naraḥ /
viṣayāḥ śatrubhūtā hi na vaśyante kathañcana // 7.132 //
kāmabaddhāḥ sadā mohabāliśā vā bhavanti te /
na tyajanti kathaṃ mūḍhā mohitāḥ svena karmaṇā // 7.133 //
yathā bahnibhayāt kaścid vahnimevopasevate /
tathā viṣayasaṃmūḍho viṣayānupasevate // 7.134 //
snāyusaṅgrathitaḥ pāśo dṛṣṭiramyo yathā bhavet /
tathā viṣayaramyo 'yaṃ pāśaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ // 7.135 //
||kāmasukhaṃ nāśāya bhavati
kiṃpākasya yathāsvādo madhurāgro mahodayaḥ /
paścād bhavati nāśāya sukhaṃ tadvadidaṃ nṛṇām // 7.136 //
pradīpasya śikhāṃ yāvat pataṅgo mohamūrchitaḥ /
patate dahyate caiva tathedaṃ sukhamiṣyate // 7.137 //
ajñātvā hi tathā bālā ramyadehasukhecchayā /
spṛśanti jvalanaṃ tadvat sukhametad bhaviṣyati // 7.138 //
||tṛṣṇāvighāta eva sukhāya jāyate
yathā ramyo vanamṛgastṛṣṇārta upadhāvati /
na ca tṛṣṇāvighāto 'sya tadidaṃ sukhamiṣyate // 7.139 //
na tṛptā na ca tṛpyanti na ca tṛptirbhaviṣyati /
viṣayaiḥ sarvadevānāṃ tasmāt kāmo na śāntaye // 7.140 //
||viṣayaiḥ pramattāḥ duḥkhamanubhavanti
pratyutpannasukhāḥ kāmā nāntakalyāṇakārakāḥ /
rañjitā viṣayairdevā vikṣiptamanasaḥ sadā // 7.141 //
nānāsaukhyapramattasya viṣayairvañcitasya ca /
samprāpte mṛtyukāle ca na śamāyāsya vidyate // 7.142 //
anukrameṇa maraṇamabhyeti tacca vidyate /
viṣayāpahatairdevaiḥ kāmavyāsaktabuddhibhiḥ // 7.143 //
||kāmā ahitakāriṇo bhavanti
jānīyādadya me devā yad duḥkhaṃ viprayogajam /
muhūrtamapi kāmeṣu na kuryāt tatra saṃsthitim // 7.144 //
||rāgāgninā dagdho vimohito jāyate
anityātmabhayāḥ kāmā nityaṃ cāhitakāriṇaḥ /
tathā vimohitān kālaḥ punastānanusevate // 7.145 //
rāgāgninā pradahayante nityaṃ devāḥ pramohitāḥ /
dahyamānāḥ punastattvaṃ praśaṃsanti punaḥ punaḥ // 7.146 //
||rathacakravatsadā bhrāntā viṣayavimohitāḥ bhavanti
viṣayeṣu na rakṣyante teṣāṃ duḥkhamiva sthitam /
traidhātukamidaṃ sarva bhrāmyate rathacakravat // 7.147 //
||gandharvanagarasadṛśāḥ kāmāḥ bhavanti
sattvā avidyayā mugdhā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhoginaḥ /
vidyudālātacakreṇa samāḥ kāmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ /
svapne gandharvanagarasadṛśā vipralambhinaḥ // 7.148 //
||pañcaskandhamatirduḥkhitastiṣṭhati
anityaduḥkhaśūnyeṣu na kuryānmatimātmavān /
pañcaskandhāsuraiḥ proktaḥ śubhai riktaḥ svabhāvataḥ // 7.149 //
anyathā viṣavad vijñaḥ kāmeṣu ca prasahyate /
sa budhaḥ pāragaḥ śāntaḥ sattvānāmanukampakaḥ // 7.150 //
nirvāṇonmukha eva doṣācchāntimadhigacchati hitvā kleśamayaṃ pāśaṃ nirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ // 7.151 //
||kāmavibhrāntasya śāntikathā vṛthā
prabhavenna ca doṣeṣu kāmacaryāratasya ca /
vibhrāntamanasastasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati? // 7.152 //
vibhrāntaṃ paśyatu mano viṣayeṣu pradhāvati /
saddharmapathavibhrānto narakeṣūpapadyate // 7.153 //
aśaktaprāptavibhraṣṭe kiṃ kāmairvidyutopamaiḥ /
kiṃpākaviṣaśastrāgnisannibhairduḥkhahetubhiḥ? // 7.154 //
||kāmāgniḥ viṣayasevanena vardhate
yathā yathā hi sevyante vardhante te tathā tathā /
avitṛptikarā hyete vahnidāhasya hetavaḥ // 7.155 //
||kāmān varjayitvaiva sukhamaśnuvate janāḥ
dāhadoṣeṇa sambhrāntāḥ ye surāḥ sukhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ /
varjayitvāśivān kāmāstataḥ saukhyaṃ bhaviṣyati // 7.156 //
||kāmāḥ vidyud guṇopamāḥ cañcalāḥ
vañcayitvā janaṃ mūḍhaṃ śāṭī kṛtyeva bandhanam /
pratyayo netracapalaḥ kāmā vidyud guṇopamāḥ // 7.157 //
uparyupari kāmā yaiḥ sevyante kāmatṛṣṇayā /
te rāgavahninā dagdhā dāhād dāhamavāpnuyāt // 7.158 //
atimūḍhatamā hyete ye surāḥ kāmamohitāḥ /
athavā ye na gacchanti yatsukhāt sukhamuttamam // 7.159 //
nirvāṇagāmino nāsti vinā muktyā kutaḥ sukham? /
tasmāt kāmānna seveta kaṣṭaḥ kāmasamāgamaḥ // 7.160 //
indriyāṇi na tṛpyante viṣayai rāgasevinaḥ /
atṛptau ca kutaḥ śarma sarvathā sampraveśate // 7.161 //
tasyāgramubhayād vetti saṃsārād duḥkhasāgarāt /
kāmān tṛṣṇāviṣayagān parityajati pāpakān // 7.162 //
||kāmodayavyayau samyagavadheyau
etāni girikūṭāni ramyāṇi vividhairdrumaiḥ /
dhyāyante tāni saṃśritya kāmānāmudayavyayau // 7.163 //
||śīlena śraddhayā ca iṣṭasādhanaṃ karttavyam
na kāmabandhanestṛptāḥ kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hi tat /
na śīlaśraddhe yeneṣṭe labhyate 'śivakāraṇam /
kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hyetat saṃsārāṭavideśakam // 7.164 //
||pāpāni parityajya sukhāvahaḥ śāntimārgaḥ sevanīyaḥ
yatra kāmavisaṃyuktaṃ bandhanaṃ vanamucyate /
yatra bhāsayate pāpād yatra śāntiḥ sukhāvahā /
tat kevalaṃ mahājñānaṃ kathyate nidhanaṃ dhanam // 7.165 //
||kāmatṛṣṇābhyāṃ vimuktaḥ śivamāpnoti
ye prasaktā na kāmeṣu tṛṣṇayā na pralobhitāḥ /
te śivaṃ sthānamāpannā na kāmāgnipraveśakāḥ // 7.166 //
||avitṛptāḥ narāḥ naśyantyeva
tṛptirnāsti sadā kāmairna kāmāḥ śāntaye smṛtāḥ /
tṛṣṇāsahāyasaṃyuktā jvalanti jvalanopamāḥ // 7.167 //
avitṛptā vinaśyanti narā devāstathoragāḥ /
te kevalaṃ praṇaṣṭā hi narakāgni pradarśakāḥ // 7.168 //
||tṛṣṇāmohitasya mṛtyuradhipatiḥ
vitarkāpahatasyāsya viṣayairvañcitasya ca /
tṛṣṇayā mohitasyaiṣa mṛtyū rājā bhaviṣyati // 7.169 //
||kāmāsaktāḥ pathyāpathyaṃ na vijānanti
saṃsaktakāmabhogeṣu pathyāpathyaṃ na vidyate /
janā vimohitāḥ sarvaiviṣayaiḥ kāmasaṃjñakaiḥ // 7.170 //
||kāmavaśānugāḥ viṣayaireva badhyante
viṣayaireva kṛṣyante ye surā mūḍhacetasaḥ /
ye (tu) buddhaguṇairyuktā na te kāmavaśānugāḥ // 7.171 //
||'dhīra' paribhāṣā
pratyutpanneṣu kāmeṣu sadoṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ /
yo na muhyati saukhyeṣu sa 'dhīra' iti kathyate // 7.172 //
||kāmapatitānāṃ surāṇāṃ sthitimāha
svapnakāyavicitreṣu jvālāmālopameṣu ca /
gandharvapuratulyeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.173 //
tṛṣṇājanakabhūteṣu vināśāntakareṣu ca /
kāntāreṣu viśāleṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.174 //
ittvareṣu trichidreṣu nadīvegopameṣu ca /
cañcaleṣvatidurgeṣu (kāmeṣu) patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.175 //
pavanoddhṛtavegormijalacandre caleṣu ca /
atātacakralokeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.176 //
samaṃ vidyullatācakramṛgatṛṣṇopameṣu ca /
phenavaccāpyasāreṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.177 //
kadalīgarbhatulyeṣu gajakarṇopameṣu ca /
nadītaraṅgavegeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.178 //
kiṃpākaphalatulyeṣu vahnisannibhajātiṣu /
māyāraśminibheṣveṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ // 7.179 //
||jñānāṅkuśena kāmo varjanīyaḥ
jñānāṅkuśena vāryante viṣayāstattvadarśibhiḥ /
ye 'muktāścapalāstīvrāḥ sarvānarthakarā matāḥ // 7.180 //
||viṣayā eva narakapātahetavaḥ
viṣayāśā ca mūḍhānāṃ saṅkalpahṛtacetasām /
mṛtyupāśo 'yamabhyeti jīvitāśā(vi)bandhakaḥ // 7.181 //
pacanti niraye kāmāḥ prāṇinaṃ laghucetasam /
na ca vindanti mūḍhā ye mohena parivañcitāḥ // 7.182 //
viṣayāścapalāḥ sarve gandharvanagaropamāḥ /
duḥkhasaṃvartakā hyete narakāḥ pañcahetavaḥ // 7.183 //
||saṅkalpajo rāgaḥ narakaṃ pātayati
saṅkalpājjāyate rāgaḥ rāgāt krodhaḥ pravartate /
krodhābhibhūtaḥ puruṣo narakānupasevate // 7.184 //
||kāmaparityāgapūrvakaṃ nirvāṇaprāptaye yateta
tasmāt kāmaṃ parityajya krodhaṃ nirvāsya paṇḍitaḥ /
mohaṃ cāpi parityajya nirvāṇābhimukho bhavet // 7.185 //
||nirvāṇapathikānāṃ kṛte śatruvadeva kāmaḥ parivarjanīyaḥ
śatruvad viṣayā jñeyā nirvāṇaṃ caiva mitravat /
pumān viśrāntaviṣayo nirvāṇamadhigacchati // 7.186 //
||kāmamalairalipta eva vimalaprakāśamāpnoti
alolupaḥ kāmamalairaliptaḥ prahīṇadoṣo hatavāṇatṛṣṇaḥ /
saṃkṣīṇadoṣo vimalaprakāśaḥ prayāti śāntiṃ svaphalopabhogī // 7.187 //
||sukhārthī kāmaṃ parityajyaiva śāntimadhigacchati
||yaḥ kāmapaṅkoddhṛtavānadoṣaḥ
sarveṣu sattveṣu sadā sukhārthī /
||sa nirmalo 'śāntamanovimuktaḥ
prāpnoti nirvāṇasukhaṃ prasahya // 7.188 //
iti kāmajugupsāvargaḥ saptamaḥ /
||(8) tṛṣṇāvargaḥ
||tṛṣṇāgnireva narakabhūtaḥ
bhavotārāya tṛṣṇāgnirjvalanaḥ śīta ucyate /
narake nārake yo 'gnistṛṣṇāgnistriṣu dhātuṣu // 8.1 //
kalpabhūto hyayaṃ vahniḥ yo 'yaṃ narakasambhavaḥ /
bahujvālākulo vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ // 8.2 //
karmakṣayād vimucyante narakāt pāpakāriṇaḥ /
triṣu dhātuṣu dahyante narāstṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ // 8.3 //
anādimati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāgniratibandhakaḥ /
tṛṣṇāgnirnarakaṃ tasmānnāgnirnarakasambhavaḥ // 8.4 //
||tṛṣṇāgniḥ śarīraṃ manaśca dahati
gātradāhaṃ paraṃ kuryānnārakeyo hutāśanaḥ /
śārīraṃ mānasaṃ dāhaṃ tṛṣṇāgniḥ kurute nṛṇām // 8.5 //
||tṛṣṇāgniḥ sāmānyāgninā viśiṣyate
tasmād viśiṣyate vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ /
nārakeyo 'samaścaiva tṛṣṇāgnirnitarāṃ smṛtaḥ // 8.6 //
||ayamagniḥ trikālasambhavaḥ
tristhānagaḥ trihetuśca trikarmaparidīpakaḥ /
trikālasambhavo jñeyastṛṣṇāgniparakastathā // 8.7 //
||tṛṣṇāgniḥ sadaiva sarvatra dāhakaḥ
rāgāgnirdahyate svarge dveṣāgnistiryage tathā /
mohāgnirdahyate pāpe tṛṣṇāgniḥ sarvadā sthitaḥ // 8.8 //
||tṛṣṇāgneḥ svarūpanirūpaṇam
mānerṣyādhūmaviśikhaḥ saṅkalpe dhanasambhavaḥ /
lobhāgnirdahate lokaṃ nāgniḥ kāmasamudbhavaḥ // 8.9 //
||tṛṣṇāgnirviṣayasevanenaiva vardhate
lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭā ye teṣāṃ śarma na vidyate /
sevito bhāvito lobho bhūya evābhivardhate // 8.10 //
||lobhasamo ripurbhuvi nāsti
yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpyānalo vardhatyanekaśaḥ /
śakyaḥ pālayituṃ(vahni) rlobhavahnirna(śakyate) // 8.11 //
cakravad bhramate loko lobhena parivañcitaḥ /
anādinidhane loke nāsti lobhasamo ripuḥ // 8.12 //
viśanti sāgarajale lobhena parivañcitāḥ /
śastrasaṅghātagahanaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃpraviśanti ca // 8.13 //
lobhahetorhi bhūpālā nāśayanti parasparam /
śastrāsibhairavaprotā yuddhayante dhanatṛṣṇayā // 8.14 //
tṛṣṇāviṣavinirmuktā lobhāṅgāravivarjitā /
samaloṣṭakāñcanā ye nirvāṇasyāntike hi te // 8.15 //
||lobhāgniḥ sarvāpekṣayā viṣamaḥ
atīvānupapannasya dhanalobhena dahyate /
na vahnirviṣamastatra lobhāgniryatra vartate // 8.16 //
||lobhaśāntiṃ vinā nirvāṇakathā vṛthā
lobhādhāraprayatnena hanyāt tān rabhasā budhaḥ /
anirvāpitalobhasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrataḥ sthitam // 8.17 //
||bhavasukhaparityāgī bhavajaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāpnoti
bhavābhilāṣiṇīṃ nāndīṃ nābhinandanti ye narāḥ /
na teṣāṃ bhavajaṃ duḥkhaṃ svapne samupavidyate // 8.18 //
||tṛṣṇābaddhān janān mṛtyuḥ śambūka iva karṣati
matsyān yathā jālabaddhān śambūkaḥ parikarṣati /
tṛṣṇābaddhāṃstathā sattvānmṛtyuḥ samupakarṣati // 8.19 //
||tṛṣṇāviṣaṃ kutrāpi na muñcati
saviṣaiḥ sāyakairviddho mṛgo yatra (pra)dhāvati /
tatra tatra viṣaṃ yāti tathā tṛṣṇāviṣaṃ nṛṇām // 8.20 //
pravāhapravahannadyā gatirgatya'nudhāvinī /
yathā nirdahate bālān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ // 8.21 //
āpātaramyā(viṣayā) vipākajvalanopamāḥ /
tasmāt tṛṣṇā vimoktavyā yadi saukhyaṃ hi rocate // 8.22 //
yathā hi vaḍiśagrastā mīnā mṛtyuvaśānugāḥ /
tathā prataptā viṣayān paridhāvanti duḥkhitāḥ // 8.23 //
||tṛṣṇāgniḥ narakādapi mahān
narakaṃ nārakeyaṃ ca tṛṣṇānihitaṃ mahat /
patanti nidhanā martyāḥ paradāropajīvinaḥ // 8.24 //
||tṛṣṇāprerito munirapi duḥkhamanubhavati
na ceṣṭitamanopāpatṛṣṇayā prerito muniḥ /
ṣaḍindriyasamudbhūto viṣayendhanadāhakaḥ // 8.25 //
||devānapi tṛṣṇāgnirdahatyeva
tṛṣṇāgnirdahate devaṃ kāyāgnirna kathañcana /
sukhāvṛtāḥ sukharatāḥ sukhe(na) parivañcitāḥ // 8.26 //
||tṛṣṇāparivañcitaḥ patanamapi nāvagacchati
patanaṃ nāvagacchanti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ /
jvālāmālākulaḥ sarvaḥ saṃsārastṛṣṇayāvṛtaḥ // 8.27 //
tṛṣṇāgninā vaśībhūtā janā gacchanti durgatim /
tṛṣṇāgnibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ suralokaḥ samantataḥ // 8.28 //
||tṛṣṇāgniḥ sadaiva vardhate
dahyate vivaśo raktaḥ kāmabhogavaśīkṛtaḥ /
yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpya jvalanaṃ saṃpravardhate // 8.29 //
tathā tathā sukhaṃ prāpya tṛṣṇāgnirvardhate nṛṇām /
parivartayate puṃsaḥ kāṣṭhāgnirdāhadīpakaḥ // 8.30 //
tṛṣṇāgnirdahate lokaṃ parihātuṃ na śakyate /
ye viśālāṃ nadīṃ tīrṇā saṅkalpakṛtabhairavīm // 8.31 //
||tṛṣṇāpāśaśūnyaḥ paramāṃ śāntimāpnoti
te gatāḥ paramāṃ śāntiṃ yān hi tṛṣṇā na bādhate /
tṛṣṇāpāśavimuktā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ // 8.32 //
nirmuktapāpakalmāṣā vītaśokā hi te budhāḥ /
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi tṛṣṇayā vañcitā narāḥ // 8.33 //
||tṛṣṇayā vañcito lokastṛṣṇāmevopāste
(na)te tyajanti(viṣayān) māyāmohavaśaṃgatāḥ /
tṛṣṇayā vañcito lokastṛṣṇāmevopasevate // 8.34 //
lavaṇodaṃ tṛṣātoyaṃ yathā pibati nārikaḥ /
na tena (tuṣyati) janturmuhuśca pariśuṣyati // 8.35 //
||duḥkhakarīṃ tṛṣṇāṃ na seveta
viṣayeṣveva tṛṣṇārtaśceṣṭate puruṣo 'dhamaḥ /
tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ na seveta sā hi tṛṣṇā durāsadā // 8.36 //
||tṛṣṇāvaśo naiva pramucyate
tṛṣṇāvaśo hi puruṣaḥ saṃsārānnaiva mucyate /
anuttamāni saukhyāni bhuktvā deveṣu jantavaḥ // 8.37 //
||tṛṣṇāpāśavikṛṣṭāḥ narakaṃ patanti
tṛṣṇāpāśavikṛṣṭāste patanti narakaṃ punaḥ /
asvatantrādikalyāṇaṃ nityaduḥkhamayaṃ kaṭu // 8.38 //
||tṛṣṇayā kadāpi tuṣṭirna bhavati
tṛṣṇāyāḥ sevanānmuktaḥ sanmārgamadhigacchati /
satṛṣṇasya kutastuṣṭirviṣayeṣu bhaviṣyati // 8.39 //
sā tṛptiryā vitṛṣṇasya vītaśokasya dehinaḥ /
evaṃ vitarkavihitāḥ pramādena ca vañcitāḥ // 8.40 //
||tṛṣṇayā devānapi narakaṃ yānti
tṛṣṇayāḥ toṣitā devāḥ patanti narakaṃ punaḥ /
viḍambaneyaṃ paramā yatsurā narakaṃ gatāḥ // 8.41 //
krīḍakāḥ paramā bhūtvā kāmasya vaśamāgatāḥ /
na codvijanti saṃsārān prāṇinaścittamohitāḥ // 8.42 //
||tṛṣṇayā duḥkhataraṃ padamāpnoti
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ /
yathā yathā sukhasyāptirvardhate jālinī tathā // 8.43 //
jālinīvahnidagdhasya narakānupakarṣati /
satṛṣṇasya vitarkā ye teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate // 8.44 //
||viṣayagāminaḥ tṛṣṇayā mṛtyumukhameva praviśanti
avitarkavitarkantu mṛtyurājo vikarṣati /
vitarkakāmavaśagāstṛṣṇāviṣayagāminaḥ // 8.45 //
||kāmāsvādapramattāḥ viṣayiṇo duḥkhinastiṣṭhanti
sukhasya bhoginaṃ dṛṣṭvā na vidvadbhistatheṣyate /
kāmāsvādapramattānāṃ prāṇināṃ viṣayārthinām // 8.46 //
||dehinaḥ tṛṣṇayā dahayante
jālinī bādhate nityaṃ yathā badhnanti dehinaḥ /
pañcālambanametattu tṛṣṇayā naiva dahayate // 8.47 //
||tṛṣṇāvimuktā vimalā bhavanti
tṛṣṇāvimuktavimalā na pāpapuragāminaḥ /
saṅkalpadoṣā kuṭilā tridoṣarajasodbhavāḥ // 8.48 //
||tṛṣṇayā saṃsārasāgare parivarte patanti janāḥ
pramādajalagambhīrāḥ strīrāgakṛtasevanāḥ /
gītatūryasvarāḥ śīghraṃ surāpānācca cañcalāḥ // 8.49 //
sañchannaviṣayā sarve manaḥ kṣiptataraṅgiṇaḥ /
tṛṣṇānadīṣu viṣame vahanti na ca gocare // 8.50 //
gāhante te ca sammūḍhāḥ surā rāgeṇa vañcitāḥ /
tridoṣakāṣṭhasaṃbhūtāḥ pramādānilavegataḥ // 8.51 //
tṛṣṇānalaḥ suragaṇān dahate na ca te viduḥ /
na kṣaṇo nāpi hi lavo na muhūrta kathañcana // 8.52 //
yā na tṛṣṇāvaśagataiḥ suraiḥ samupabhujyate /
tṛṣṇābhūmiriyaṃ kāṣṭhā vitarkajalasambhṛtā // 8.53 //
||tṛṣṇāsarpadagdhaḥ kālavaśīkṛto bhavati
yasmin krīḍanti vivaśāḥ devāḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ /
cittādinā pracaṇḍena tṛṣṇāviṣavisarpiṇā // 8.54 //
daṣṭānupañcaśīrṣeṇa kiṃ vṛthā vilapasyatha /
tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ pañcatīrthasamudbhavā // 8.55 //
tṛṣṇāmohendrajālena viprakīrṇena sarvadā /
tathā prapañcitā devā yathā na śubhabhāginaḥ // 8.56 //
||tṛṣṇāviṣayaghṛtasikto vardhata eva
nendriyāṇi sadā kāmaistṛpyanti hi kathañcana /
saṃvardhate tathā tṛṣṇā ghṛtasikto yathānalaḥ // 8.57 //
||tṛṣṇayā vividhāsu yoniṣu janāḥ bhramanti
nānāvidhaiḥ sukhaireṣā jālinī lokanāśinī /
narakapretatiryakṣu bhrāmayantī narān sadā // 8.58 //
||vītatṛṣṇaḥ nirmuktabandhanaḥ paramāṃ gatimāpnoti
mṛtyūpapattidolāyāṃ śliṣyante bāliśāḥ janāḥ /
suśīlāvītatṛṣṇāśca gatāste paramāṃ gatim // 8.59 //
nirmuktabandhanā dhīrā gataśokā gatavyathāḥ /
sukhaṃ prāpnuvanti nityaṃ ye na tṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ /
janmaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairna te vidhyanti sūrayaḥ // 8.60 //
||tṛṣṇāvisṛṣṭiḥ jñānāya pravartayati
yeṣāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsu jñāneṣu vihitaṃ manaḥ /
animitte mano yeṣāṃ visṛṣṭā ye ca tṛṣṇayā /
te vītamalakāntārāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam // 8.61 //
||tṛṣṇāmohapramattāḥ bhave bhave bhramanti
tṛṣṇāmohapramattā ye ratisaukhyāstathaiva ca /
mohitāste devagaṇā bhramiṣyanti bhave bhave // 8.62 //
||aharniśaṃ tṛṣṇā tāpayati
kuṭṭanavyavahārā ye paricittāpahāriṇaḥ /
avidyābahulā ye vā nityaṃ dāhābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ /
na rātrau na divā teṣāṃ hṛdayaṃ suprasīdati // 8.63 //
||lobhābhibhūtāḥ tuṣāgnikalpā bhavanti
lobhābhibhūtamanasāṃ parivittābhikāṅkṣiṇām /
teṣāṃ tuṣāgnikalpānāṃ viśvasenna svabhāvataḥ // 8.64 //
||viṣayendhana sarpād bhayamevocitam
bibheti hi naraḥ sarvaḥ sarpādiva viṣendhanāt /
lobhena viṣayeṇaivābhibhūtāste narā bhṛśam // 8.65 //
||tṛṣṇāvaśagāḥ vividhāṃ yoniṃ labhante
te mṛtā narakaṃ yānti pretayoniṃ tathaiva ca /
tasmādapi vinirmuktā narakād vahnisammukhāt // 8.66 //
||ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ nityaṃ duḥkhabhāgino bhavanti
pañcajanmaśatānyete bhavanti parikāṅkṣiṇaḥ /
vivarṇā dīnavadanā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ /
bhavanti manujāḥ sarve lobhopahatacetasaḥ // 8.67 //
||vivekasampannāḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ labhante
prahīṇalobhā ye santi nityaṃ jñānābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ /
buddhimantaḥ sadā santaḥ te gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim /
nirvāṇahṛdayā vītalobhamohāḥ sadā narāḥ // 8.68 //
||lobhākṛṣṭasya vinipātaḥ
lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭasya vinipāto dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ /
kriyamāṇo dhruvaṃ loko vardhate sa muhurmuhuḥ // 8.69 //
śuṣkendhanaṃ samādāya yathā vahniḥ pravardhate /
dhanatṛṣṇāratāḥ sattvāḥ dhanopārjanatatparāḥ // 8.70 //
mṛtyukāle samutpanne tyajanti vivaśā dhanam /
yacca tatsambhavaṃ yogāt tat sarva na vinaśyati // 8.71 //
||lobhātmā ghoraṃ narakaṃ yāti
tena vittena lobhātmā nīyate narakaṃ bhṛśam /
anyaistadbhujyate vittaṃ sa tu pāpena lipyate // 8.72 //
prayānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ paścāttāpena dahyate /
anartho hyartharūpeṇa sukharūpeṇa vā sukham // 8.73 //
||lobhatyāgaṃ prājñaḥ kuryāt
amitraṃ mitrarūpeṇa lobho 'yaṃ hṛdi vartate /
na lobhaṃ saṃśrayet prājño lobhāgnirdahyate sadā // 8.74 //
||lobhadagdhāḥ narakagāmino bhavanti
tena dagdhā bhṛśaṃ sattvāḥ paścānnarakagāminaḥ /
lokasādhāraṇā hyete vibhavāḥ sukhavarjitāḥ // 8.75 //
||tṛṣṇābhayavimuktireva śreyaskarī
teṣāmarthe kathaṃ pāpa kriyate mandabuddhibhiḥ /
tṛṣṇābhayavimuktasya nirāśasya hi sarvataḥ // 8.76 //
vītakāṅkṣasya dhīrasya nityaṃ padamavasthitam /
sampattau dhābate loko vipattau nāvabudhyate // 8.77 //
||sampattiḥ kṣayāntā
vipadantā hi sampattiḥ kṣayāntaṃ divasaṃ yathā /
yathā tiṣṭhati sampattiḥ vipattiḥ pāpikā tathā // 8.78 //
||kāmabhogairdevā api narakaṃ yānti
avitṛptasya kāmebhyastṛṣṇayā paridahyate /
yasyeṣṭāḥ sampado nityaṃ sukhaṃ cābhimataṃ sadā // 8.79 //
jani nāśayate tāsāṃ tṛṣṇā naṣṭā sukhāvahā /
te devā narakaṃ yānti kāmabhogaistathārpitāḥ // 8.80 //
analāceṣṭitaṃ sarva tad vadanti tathāgatāḥ /
manuṣyā yacca narakaṃ prayā(nti) śataśastathā // 8.81 //
||vimugdhāḥ yati jīvanaṃ nāvagacchanti
ceṣṭitaṃ tad viśālāyāḥ yoṣikāyā vidurbudhāḥ /
vimohitā na vindanti tvaritaṃ svalpajīvitam // 8.82 //
||tṛṣṇayā sukṛtāni vinaśyanti
sukṛtāni ca naśyanti tṛṣṇā naiva vinaśyati /
bhave bhave gatā satvāḥ na vindanti śubhāśubham // 8.83 //
śubhasya phalameveṣṭaṃ yat surāḥ paribhuñjate /
aśubhasya tathā dṛṣṭamasukhaṃ vinipātajam // 8.84 //
||śubhāśubhaprahīṇā eva jarāmaraṇarahitā bhavanti
śubhāśubhaprahīṇā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ /
te gatāḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam // 8.85 //
||tṛṣṇānadīparikṣiptaḥ janaḥ kimapi nāvagacchati
pañcāraṃ bhavacakraṃ tat tṛṣṇānābhipuraḥsaram /
nadīrāgaparikṣiptaṃ na ca loko 'vabudhyate // 8.86 //
doṣāvartatarā jñeyā saṅkalpamakarākulāḥ /
tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ na ca loko 'vabudhyate // 8.87 //
||tṛṣṇā triṣu kāleṣu vañcikā
trikāle vañcanī tṛṣṇā nityamajñānakāriṇī /
na tasyāṃ viśvased dhīmān saṃsārabandhanā hi sā // 8.88 //
||tṛṣṇā lokabandhanabhūtā
mitravad dṛśyate kāle śatruvacca nikṛntati /
na tasyāṃ viśvaset prājñaḥ sā hi lokasya bandhanam // 8.89 //
śakyaṃ hi bandhanaṃ chettumāyasaṃ dāruvattathā /
na tṛṣṇābandhanaṃ chettuṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣibhiḥ // 8.90 //
yasyeṣṭo bandhabhedo 'yaṃ yasyeṣṭaṃ sukhamavyayam /
sa tṛṣṇayā vimuktaḥ (syāt)prajñāśo (dhanakṛd) bhavet // 8.91 //
||jñānena tṛṣṇāvṛkṣasya chedanaṃ karttavyam
jñānālokaḥ sukhāloko duḥkhaṃ tṛṣṇātamaḥsmṛtam /
tasmādālokamāsthāya tamo nudati paṇḍitaḥ // 8.92 //
jñānakhaḍgena tīkṣṇena tṛṣṇāvṛkṣaṃ nikṛntati /
nikṛttavṛkṣaḥ (sa) naraḥ sukhaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam // 8.93 //
doṣeṇa bahulā hyeṣā nadī prasravaṇākulā /
doṣā netānahitvā (na) bhavānmuñcati paṇḍitaḥ // 8.94 //
||prajñānāvamāśritya tṛṣṇānadyāḥ pāraṃ gacchati
tṛṣṇānadīṃ tripathagāṃ pramādāvartadustarām /
prajñānāvaṃ samāśritya pāraṃ gacchantyanāmayam // 8.95 //
mahecchatāmahacchatraṃ yena cāyānti bāliśāḥ /
tasmānmahecchatā badhyā tvayeyaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā // 8.96 //
||mahecchaiva hṛdayavraṇabhūtā
mahecchatāvraṇastīvro hṛdaye yasya jāyate /
na rātrau na divā tasya sukhaṃ bhavati lobhinaḥ // 8.97 //
saṅkalpe tu na sambhūtaḥ tṛṣṇāvāyusamīritaḥ /
mahecchatāmayo vahnirdahate hṛdayaṃ nṛṇām // 8.98 //
||lobhenātmano 'hitaṃ kurvanti janāḥ
lobhenāveṣṭitamanāḥ puruṣo laghucetasā /
jīvitānyapi sārāṇi jahāti dhanatṛṣṇayā // 8.99 //
pāpāni hi ca karmāṇi kurvanti puruṣāḥ kṣitau /
dhanalābhena tat sarva pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ // 8.100 //
ye sāhasaṃ na kurvanti viśanti jvalanaṃ ca yat /
tat sarva lobhadoṣeṇa kurvantyahitamātmanaḥ // 8.101 //
śastrānilāni duḥkhāni vividhāni ca (sarvataḥ) /
viśanti (vai) narā mūḍhā lobhastatra hi kāraṇam // 8.102 //
hṛdayastho manovahnirnityaṃ bahvicchatāṃ nṛṇām /
alpecchatayā (hi) hṛcchāntirbhavatilābhinaḥ // 8.103 //
yathāgnirindhanenaiva praśāntimadhigacchati /
tathā vahvicchatāṃ nṛṇāṃ dhanairvṛddhiḥ prajāyate // 8.104 //
||alpecchataiva sukham
bhūpālā (hi) dhanaistṛptāḥ koṭiśo nidhanaṃ gatāḥ /
yāsyanti cānye nidhanaṃ tasmādalpecchatā sukham // 8.105 //
||tṛṣṇāvihīna eva sukhamāpnoti
duḥkhaṃ vahvicchatā nṛṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ /
(heyā sarvaprayatnena) idamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ /
eṣa panthāḥ śivaḥ śreṣṭho yena tṛṣṇā vaśīkṛtā // 8.106 //
// iti tṛṣṇāvargo 'ṣṭamaḥ //
||(9) strījugupsāvargaḥ
||striya evānarthamūlam
striyo mūlaṃ (hi) pāpasya dhananāśasya sarvathā /
svahite ye na niratāḥ kutasteṣāṃ bhavet sukham // 9.1 //
anarthakarmaratayaḥ śāṭhyerṣyābahulāstriyaḥ /
lokadvayavināśāya puruṣāṇāmavasthitāḥ // 9.2 //
nityaṃ sarāgakuśalā nityaṃ tadvacanāḥ parāḥ /
anyacca hṛdaye tāsāṃ kathayantyanyadeva vā // 9.3 //
āpātamadhurāḥ sūkṣmāḥ vipāke vajracetasaḥ /
nopakāreṇa satkāraṃ smaranti laghucetasaḥ // 9.4 //
||striyo vidyutsvabhāvahṛdayā aticañcalāḥ
nāśayitvā priyaśataṃ smarantyekaṃ hi vipriyam /
vidyutsvabhāvahṛdayāḥ striyaḥ pāpasya bhūmayaḥ // 9.5 //
||strīṇāṃ nāśasādhakatvapradarśanam
strīhetunāśamicchanti puruṣā vakracetasaḥ /
strīvināśo vināśo drāgiha loke paratra ca // 9.6 //
||strīdarśanamevāgnivaddahati
evaṃ tu sarvaviṣayāḥ strīdarśanamihaikajam /
abhibhūya sarvaviṣayān nāryagnijvalanaṃ mahat // 9.7 //
||strīdoṣapradarśanapūrvakaṃ nārījugupsāsamīkṣaṇam
saṃśleṣādapi viśleṣaḥ smaraṇāt kathanādapi /
strīṇāṃ dāhasamuttho 'yaṃ vahnirantarjahāsakaḥ // 9.8 //
rāgeṇa saha jāyante nityaṃ vai dāruṇāḥ striyaḥ /
dānena saha jāyante yathā loke hutāśanāḥ // 9.9 //
na bhavet tādṛśo dāho yo 'yaṃ vahnisamudbhavaḥ /
yādṛśaḥ strīmado hyasti dehināṃ hṛdayodbhavaḥ // 9.10 //
sarvalokavināśāya sarvadharmakṣayāya ca /
hetavo narakasyaitāḥ striyaḥ proktā maharṣibhiḥ // 9.11 //
mukhato madhurāmarṣā hṛdayena viṣopamāḥ /
anavasthitasauhārdā nāsāṃ kaścit priyo naraḥ // 9.12 //
muhūrtena priyastāsāṃ muhūrtena tathāpriyaḥ /
anavasthitasauhārdāścañcalā kṣaṇikopamāḥ // 9.13 //
vañcanāhetukuśalā nityaṃ kāryaparāyaṇāḥ /
nityaṃ saṃyogamanaso nityaṃ mānaparāyaṇāḥ // 9.14 //
devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ /
na bandhabhūtā yādṛśyaḥ striyaḥ kālaviṣopamāḥ // 9.15 //
nopakāraṃ smarantyetā na kuśalaṃ nāpi vikramam /
anavasthitacittāśca vāyuvegasamāḥ striyaḥ // 9.16 //
bhavanti sampado yatra rakṣyante yatra yoṣitaḥ /
vyasaneṣu viraktāstu tyajanti puruṣaṃ dhruvam // 9.17 //
yaṃ yaṃ gacchanti puruṣaṃ rakṣyante tatra yoṣitaḥ /
śīghraṃ śīghraṃ naraṃ hyetāstyajanti puruṣaṃ sthitam // 9.18 //
yathā hi bhramarī puṣpaṃ śuṣkaṃ tyajati sarvadā /
tathā vittena rahitaṃ puruṣaṃ tyajati priyā // 9.19 //
nistriṃśahṛdayāḥ krūrāścañcalāstamasāvṛtāḥ /
striyaḥ puruṣanāśāya jātāḥ kenāpi hetunā // 9.20 //
devānāṃ bandhanaṃ nāma yathā strībandhanaṃ matam /
strībandhananibaddhāstu patanti narakaṃ punaḥ // 9.21 //
etadagraṃ hi rāgāṇāṃ yo rāgaḥ strīsamudbhavaḥ /
strīrāgadagdhamanasaṃ paścād dahati pāvakaḥ // 9.22 //
pratyakṣāṇyapi karmāṇi rāgaiścāpahataḥ pumān /
na vetti mūḍhahṛdayaḥ strīrāgeṇa vimohitaḥ // 9.23 //
viśvāsya viṣaye puruṣaṃ bad dhvā priyamanekaśaḥ /
tyajanti vittanāśena tvacaṃ yadvadbhujaṅgamāḥ // 9.24 //
sarvopāyabhṛtā nāryaḥ sarvaśaḥ paripālitāḥ /
na śakyāḥ svavaśīkarttuṃ striyaḥ paramadāruṇāḥ // 9.25 //
āsāṃ sarvasvabhāvānāṃ nārīṇāṃ calacetasām /
na yāyājjātu viśvāsaṃ pumān dhīreṇa cetasā // 9.26 //
strīvidheyāstu ye martyā nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇaḥ /
paścimadarśanaṃ teṣāṃ suraloke bhaviṣyati // 9.27 //
pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa vipralubdhāḥ samantataḥ /
vindanti vyasane duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati // 9.28 //
imāstāścañcalā nāryo yāsāṃ rāgaḥ kṛtastvayā /
tā bhavantaṃ parityajya punaranyaṃ tato gatāḥ // 9.29 //
dvidhā hi prakṛtiryāsāṃ (yoṣitāṃ) sahacāriṇī /
bhūyo 'bhiyanti puruṣaṃ vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca // 9.30 //
mṛgavanmohayantyetāḥ puruṣaṃ rāgamohitam /
paścāt (tu) vyasane prāpte tyajanti laghucetasaḥ // 9.31 //
nopakāraṃ na satkāraṃ na priyāṇi na santatim /
smaranti yoṣitastīvrā vyasane samupasthite // 9.32 //
mlānaṃ puṣpaṃ yathā tyaktvā bhramaro 'nyatra dhāvati /
tathā hi vyasane prāpte tyajanti khalu yoṣitaḥ // 9.33 //
anapekṣitasauhārdāścañcalāśca raṇapriyāḥ /
bhavanti yoṣitaḥ sarvā viṣamiśraṃ yathā madhu // 9.34 //
mohayanti narān kāmairvākyaiścāpi viśeṣataḥ /
na teṣāṃ viśvaseddhīmān puruṣo dhīramānasaḥ // 9.35 //
ābhirvimohitāḥ kiṃ vā raṃjitāḥ puruṣāḥ svataḥ /
na kurvanti hitaṃ vākyaṃ yathā muṣṇikagāmikam // 9.36 //
devāsuranarān yakṣān piśācoragarākṣasān /
indrajālamayā nāryo vañcayanti viśeṣataḥ // 9.37 //
etadagrañca pāśānāṃ yadidaṃ strīmayaṃ dṛḍham /
anena baddhāḥ puruṣā bhramanti bhavacārake // 9.38 //
na kaścit pāśapāśo 'yaṃ hṛtpāśo yoṣitaḥ param /
hṛtpāśabandhanairbaddhāḥ puruṣā duḥkhamohitāḥ // 9.39 //
dahayate chidyate pāśasstrīmayastu na dahayate /
narakapretatiryakṣu gacchantamanugacchati // 9.40 //
mūrtimān badhyate kāyaḥ pāśena mahatā tathā /
amūrtigaṃ cittamidaṃ strīpāśena tu badhyate // 9.41 //
(na) dṛśyate pāśamanyaṃ yena badhnanti yoṣitaḥ /
abhijñeyamapramāṇaṃ strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ mahat // 9.42 //
anenāpātaramyeṇa (duḥkha) mokṣeṇa sarvadā /
pāśena baddhāḥ puruṣā na mucyante bhavārṇavāt // 9.43 //
ṣaḍindriyāṇi badhnāti pāśo yaḥ strīmayo mahān /
pāśastu kāyamevaikaṃ kaścit badhnāti vā na vā // 9.44 //
bandhanaṃ na dṛḍhaṃ hīdaṃ mokṣavārya ṣaḍāyasam /
saṃraktacittabhoge hi mandabuddhernarasya ca // 9.45 //
snāyuyantreṇa baddhāsu vistṛtakarmabhūmiṣu /
tīkṣṇaraktāsinā yukto maraṇārthamihāgataḥ // 9.46 //
||strīṇāṃ daurguṇyam
vañcanācchalakūṭāsu rabhasā nu viśeṣataḥ /
cañcalo bhrāntacittāsu bhrāntastvaṅgakṣaṇāriṣu // 9.47 //
vibhrānto bhrāntakathitairbhūṣaṇānāṃ tathā svanaiḥ /
haranti puruṣaṃ kṣipraṃ vañcanākuśalāḥ striyaḥ // 9.48 //
nānāvidheṣu puṣpeṣu yathā carati ṣaṭ padaḥ /
nānāvidheṣu martyeṣu tathemāścañcalāḥ striyaḥ // 9.49 //
yathā madhurikā pītvā puṣpamanyatra gacchati /
tathā puruṣamāpīyaḥ prayānti rabhasaṃ striyaḥ // 9.50 //
arthādāneṣu kuśalāḥ kruddhā nityaṃ durāsadāḥ /
vañcayitvā naraṃ śīghramanyatra saṃprayānti tāḥ // 9.51 //
sādhyamāyāpraharaṇāḥ kālakūṭaviṣopamāḥ /
striyaḥ puruṣaghātinyaścāturyeṣu vyavasthitāḥ // 9.52 //
vāyvākāśānalā yadvan na śaktā grathituṃ naraiḥ /
tathopāyaśatairnāryo (na) śaktā rakṣituṃ naraiḥ // 9.53 //
anarthavyādhimṛtyūnāṃ duṣkṛtānāñca karmaṇām /
hetubhūtāḥ paraṃ nāryo mokṣacaryābadhasya ca // 9.54 //
yadanekaprakāreṣu śaṭheṣu pāpakarmasu /
(patanti) manujā loke tatra hetuḥ parastriyaḥ // 9.55 //
na bālayauvanenaiva vārdhakyenaiva śāmyati /
cāpalyaṃ sahajaṃ strīṇāṃ bhāskarasya yathā prabhā // 9.56 //
anityaṃ sauhṛdaṃ tāsāṃ dīptānāmarciṣāṃ kaṇaiḥ /
vairañca śāśvataṃ tāsāmaśmanāṃ ca yathā vraṇaiḥ // 9.57 //
dhanahīne virajyante dhanayuktā bhavanti ca /
yāvadartha striyastāvadarthahīne kutaḥ striyaḥ? // 9.58 //
na sevābhiścadānena nopakāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ /
svīkarttuṃ na striyaḥ śakyāḥ jvalanopamacetasaḥ // 9.59 //
yathā naro 'nukūlaśca chandakarttā yathā yathā /
tathā tathā striyastasya vañcanākuśalāḥ param // 9.60 //
puṣpacchatro yathā sarpo bhasmacchatro yathā nalaḥ /
rūpacchannaṃ tathā cittamāsāṃ bhavati yoṣitām // 9.61 //
viṣavṛkṣe yathā puṣpaṃ dṛṣṭiramyaṃ na śāntaye /
viṣavṛkṣa (samā) nāryaḥ parivarjyāḥ samantataḥ // 9.62 //
nārīṇāṃ darśanākāṃkṣī viṣayesu ca tatparaḥ /
naro na sukhabhogāya (haya) smilloke na cāpare // 9.63 //
nāgninā na ca śastreṇa na balena na jantubhiḥ /
strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ hetuḥ śakyate na durāsadam // 9.64 //
doṣajālamidaṃ (sūtraṃ)strīmayaṃ carate bhuvi /
yastrīvivarjito dhīmān asmilloke mahīyate // 9.65 //
yathā bhūtairmanuṣyāṇāṃ svakarmotthāpane na ca /
tathā striyo hi rakṣanti viṣamārtha tyajanti ca // 9.66 //
gatārthavibhavaṃ bhūyo varjitaṃ svena karmaṇā /
devaṃ samīkṣya capalāḥ striyo naiva prabhāvikāḥ // 9.67 //
||strīsukhaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅguram
kṣaṇabhaṅgamidaṃ saukhyamadhigatamavasthitam /
catvāryetāni duḥkhāni sevitāni nṛbhiḥ sadā // 9.68 //
||strī viṣāgnisadṛśā
tasmāt tāni vivarjyāni viṣāgnisadṛśāni hi /
yaḥ kaściccapalo janturyaśca doṣodbhavaḥ sadā // 9.69 //
tasmāt parisamāviṣṭāḥ striyaḥ kāraṇavatsalāḥ /
na sūryastamaso heturnāgniḥ śītasya kāraṇam // 9.70 //
na strīṇāṃ sauhṛdaṃ citte svalpamapyavatiṣṭhate /
yathā sthirā bhūmiriyaṃ yathā vāyuḥ sadā calaḥ // 9.71 //
||striyaḥ doṣameva smaranti
tathā strīṇāṃ kṛtaṃ nāsti doṣamayyaḥ sadā smṛtāḥ /
ciraprayatnāḥ puruṣaiḥ lobhitā bahuśaḥ striyaḥ // 9.72 //
tyajanti vyasane prāpte śuṣkaṃ sara ivāśugāḥ /
nordhvagāḥ sarito dṛṣṭā nāśmano gatiriṣyate // 9.73 //
girīṇāṃ gamanaṃ nāsti strīṇāṃ naivāsti sauhṛdam /
vapukarti sadā nṛṇāṃ dharmārthayaśasāṃ tathā // 9.74 //
yoniścānarthajālasya doṣāṇāmudbhavasya ca /
bhaved vajramayī mṛdvī tyajed (rātrau yathā) ravim // 9.75 //
na strī tyajedasādhyāni janmāpekṣā viśeṣataḥ /
nopacārakriyā dānapriyavākyāpalāpanaiḥ // 9.76 //
svīkartuṃ na striyaḥ śakyā jvalanopamacetasaḥ /
sukheṣu samatāṃ yānti vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca // 9.77 //
upakārāṃśca vismṛtya doṣamekaṃ smaranti tāḥ /
vanopavanaśaileṣu bhuktvā sukhamanekaśaḥ // 9.78 //
||strī lokasya bandhanam
saṃprāpte vyasane tīvre striya paribhavanti hi /
lokasya bandhanaṃ nāryo vañcanākṛtivardhikāḥ // 9.79 //
adhamāḥ vinipātānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ cāspadaṃ (bahu) /
sarvalokavināśāya vaśīkurvanti tṛṣṇayā // 9.80 //
yathā strībandhanamidaṃ durviṣahyaṃ kṛtaṃ mahat /
yadidaṃ bandhanaṃ loke kāmarāgamayaṃ mahat // 9.81 //
||strīvarjanameva śreyaṣkaram
tathā cānyaprayatnena vicārya upalabhyate /
vaśīkurvanti tā (nāryaḥ) kāmavāṇairanekaśaḥ // 9.82 //
svalpaiḥ parājitaṃ kṛtvā kāmasya vaśagāḥ striyaḥ /
rāgerṣyāśāṭhyabhūmīnāṃ vidyuccañcalacetasām // 9.83 //
lobhāhaṅkārayonīnāṃ na viśvāsyāḥ kathañcana /
śastrāgnisadṛśāstīkṣṇāḥ kāmapāśaparātmanaḥ // 9.84 //
svabhraprapātaviṣamaṃ gaṃbhīrasamacetasām /
parābhidrohamāyendrajālatadgatamānasān // 9.85 //
akālamṛtyuvajrāgnikālakūṭasamātmanām /
anekadoṣasambhārananditānāmanekaśaḥ // 9.86 //
yadi śīlalavaḥ kaścit strīṇāṃ manasi vartate /
cireṇa dahate vahniḥ sa spṛṣṭāḥ pavaneritaḥ // 9.87 //
strīdarśanasamucchreyamātraṃ dahati pāvakaḥ /
tasmāt striyo vivarjyāḥ syuḥ yadicchet sukhamuttamam // 9.88 //
etat sarva paraṃ loke nārīṇāṃ varjanaṃ sadā /
yadṛcchājālinīhetuṃ yaḥ icched bhūtimātmanaḥ // 9.89 //
ya icchati nivṛttiṃ tu sa naraḥ strīṃ vivarjayet /
sukhāsaktastathārtho (ca) kusīdaścañcalaḥ śaṭhaḥ // 9.90 //
pāpasevī sumṛṣṭāśī naro bhadraṃ na paśyati /
udyukto vīryavān dhīro dhārmikaḥ strīṃ vivarjayet /
dakṣo hetuphalaśraddho naraḥ kalyāṇavān bhavet // 9.91 //
// iti strījugupsāvargo navamaḥ //
||(10) madyajugupsāvargaḥ
||madyapānavarṇanasādhanapradarśanam
madyapānaṃ na seveta madyaṃ hi viṣamuttamam /
naśyanti kuśalā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt // 10.1 //
yaḥ sevate sadā madyaṃ tasya buddhirasaṃsthitā /
balabuddhī na dharmo 'sti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet // 10.2 //
nāśānāmuttamaṃ nāśaṃ madyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ /
tasmānmadyaṃ na seveta (madyaṃ) nāśayate naram // 10.3 //
aniṣṭāḥ pāpakā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt /
bhavanti tasmād viṣavanmadyapānaṃ vivarjayet // 10.4 //
dhanakṣayaṃ pāpakaraṃ kausīdyakaramuttamam /
madyapānasthitā doṣāḥ tasmāt tat parivarjayet // 10.5 //
rāgasyoddīpanaṃ madyaṃ krodhasyāpi tathaiva ca /
mohasyoddīpakaṃ bhūyastasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet // 10.6 //
madyamūlamanarthasya hāsasya narakasya ca /
sarvendriyavināśānāṃ hetubhūtaṃ hyanarthakam // 10.7 //
atiharṣābhidhānasya śokasya ca bhayasya ca /
vāgdoṣasyātidamyasya pāruṣyasyāspadaṃ hi tat // 10.8 //
madyenākṣiptamanasaḥ puruṣāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ /
kāryākārya na vindanti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet // 10.9 //
madyakṣipto hi puruṣo jīvannapi mṛto mataḥ /
ya icchejjīvitaṃ saukhyaṃ sa madyaṃ varjayet sadā // 10.10 //
||madyaṃ sarvadoṣāspadam
sarvadoṣāspadaṃ madyaṃ sarvānarthakaraṃ sadā /
sarvapāpeṣu sopānaṃ tamasāmālayo mahān // 10.11 //
||madyena pretaloke narake vā patanam
madyena narakaṃ yānti pretalokaṃ tathaiva ca /
tiryakṣu yānti puruṣā madyadoṣeṇa vañcitāḥ // 10.12 //
viṣādapi viṣaṃ madyaṃ narakānnarakaṃ tathā /
vyādhīnāṃ ca paraṃ vyādhirmadyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ // 10.13 //
||madyena hānipradarśanam
buddhīndriyavināśāya dharmaratnaṃ kṣayāya ca /
yo 'tirekaparaṃ madyaṃ brahmacaryabadhāya ca // 10.14 //
madyena laghutāṃ yānti pārthivā śāstracakṣuṣaḥ /
kiṃ punaḥ prākṛtā martyā madyapānavilambitāḥ // 10.15 //
||madyasya vināśakaratvam
kuṭhāraḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ hrīvināśakaraṃ param /
madyaṃ niṣevitaṃ martyairvināśāyopakalpyate // 10.16 //
||madyena jñānājñānavivekaśūnyapradarśanam
na jñānaṃ nāpi vijñānaṃ na kāryāṇi na ca kriyām /
jānīte puruṣaḥ sarva madyena hṛtacetasā // 10.17 //
||madyasevanasya paritāpasādhanam
akasmāt tapyate janturakasmāt paritapyate /
bhavatyakasmāt pāpī (ca) yo madyamanusevate // 10.18 //
||madyasya buddhisammohajanakatvam
buddhisammohajanakaṃ lokadvayavināśakam /
vahniśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ madyamekaṃ vyavasthitam // 10.19 //
||madyasya kimpākatvam
abhyāse madhuraṃ madyaṃ vipāke paramaṃ kaṭu /
kimpākādapi kimpākaṃ madyamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ // 10.20 //
||narakasya sādhanaṃ madyam
na madye viśvaseddhīmān naraṃ vakṣyati māmiti /
śītasparśa vipākoṣṇaṃ madyaṃ narakagāmikam // 10.21 //
sampattau vyasanaṃ madyaṃ devānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ /
yathā yathā sukhā prītistannāśe vyasanaṃ tathā // 10.22 //
madyapānamadonmattāḥ sattvā mohavaśānugāḥ /
sākṣyamohamayaṃ pānaṃ pibanti rasatṛṣṇayā // 10.23 //
madyaṃ mohamayaṃ pāna pītvā kālena coditāḥ /
nākāt pratyakṣanarakaṃ tasmāt madyaṃ na saṃspṛśet // 10.24 //
||darśanātpānācca madyapānaṃ mohajanakam
darśanāt sparśanāt pānāta madyaṃ mohayate naram /
tasmāt sa madyapānaṃ ca dūrataḥ parivarjayet // 10.25 //
darśanājjāyate lobhaḥ sparśanād gandhasambhavaḥ /
gandhād rasābhilāṣaśca rasanādadhamā matiḥ // 10.26 //
||manīṣiṇaḥ madyasevanātpatanti
naikasarvādhamaṃ nyāsaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ /
nāmarūpaniṣedhāya yathā madyaṃ niṣevitam // 10.27 //
||madyapānaphalasūcanam
vāgbhrāmayati mastiṣkaṃ cakṣuṣīdhvanireva ca /
sambhrāntivimatirmūḍho na kiñcit pratipadyate // 10.28 //
||striyo 'pi madyapāyinamupahasanti
striyo 'pyupahasantīmaṃ puruṣaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi /
niśceṣṭaṃ kāṣṭhasadṛśaṃ niścalaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi // 10.29 //
||madyapānaṃ maraṇādapi nikṛṣṭataram
sambhāvitasya maraṇaṃ madyapānaṃ prakīrtyate /
hālāhalādabhyadhikaṃ kārāvāsādhikaṃ ca tat // 10.30 //
||madyapānavarjanaṃ śreyaskaram
ādīnavāśca ṣaṭ triṃśanmadyapānādavasthitāḥ /
tasmādādīnavo jñeyaḥ sa hi tad varjayet sadā // 10.31 //
||madyapānaṃ viduṣo 'pi jantoḥ malinīkaraṇāya bhavati
atijātasya viduṣo malinīkaraṇaṃ mahat /
kāśapuṣpasamaṃ jantuṃ kurute laghusattvaram // 10.32 //
||viṣayānaladagdhaḥ kāryākāryaśūnyo bhavati
pramādauhyati magnānāṃ viṣayairapahṛṣyate /
madyapānena bhūyaśca manovyāmohakāriṇā // 10.33 //
viṣayānaladagdhasya kāryākāryamajānataḥ /
vanopavanalabdhasya madyapānasya kiṃ punaḥ // 10.34 //
||madyapānaṃ mohāya pāpāya jāyate
rasena śobhanaṃ madyaṃ pariṇāmena dāruṇam /
pariṇāmaphalaṃ pāpaṃ narakeṣūpapadyate // 10.35 //
pītaṃ janayate mohaṃ mohāt pāpeṣu rakṣyate /
saṃraktahṛdayo bālo narakānupadhāvati // 10.36 //
||madyapānamadhamatvasādhanam
prakarṣa janayatyādau vipāke dainyamuttamam /
tṛṭ chedaṃ kurute cāsau paścāddāhaṃ sudāruṇam // 10.37 //
tad buddhiṃ nāśayatyādau paścānnāśayate sukham /
tasmāt sa puruṣo dhīro yo madyaṃ nānusevate // 10.38 //
||madyaniṣeviṇo vihagasadṛśā bhavanti
vihagaiḥ sadṛśaṃ yānti puruṣā madyasevinaḥ /
tulyaṃ vyāmohajanakaṃ madyaṃ mohamahāviṣam // 10.39 //
||vimohitā durgatimadhigacchanti
yairmadyaṃ viṣavad dṛṣṭaṃ tairdṛṣṭaṃ padamuttamam /
yaistu tad virasaṃ pītaṃ pītaṃ tāmra (ka) lohitam // 10.40 //
niṣpratīkārakarmāṇi yaḥ karoti vimohitaḥ /
madyapānasamāviṣṭaḥ so 'nte gacchati durgatim // 10.41 //
||madyapānasevināṃ nāśo bhavati
ekatra sarvapāpāni madyapāna (niṣevaṇam) /
yasmānnāśayate (madyaṃ) cittamūlaśca saṃvaraḥ // 10.42 //
||madyapāyī naṣṭadharmo bhavati
naikāṅgitā hi cittasya na dharmāṇāṃ vicāraṇā /
yaḥ pā(pa)nirato bhikṣurbhavenmadyaniṣevaṇāt // 10.43 //
madyenākṣiptamanaso kuśalasya ca ghātakaḥ /
naṣṭadharmasya sattvasya nāyaṃ loko na cāparaḥ // 10.44 //
īryyāpathaṃ na jānāti na kālaṃ nāpi deśanām /
saddharmato viruddhaśca tucchaṃ kimapi bhāṣate // 10.45 //
svayaṃ tāvanna jānāti kimidaṃ kathyate mayā /
vākpāruṣyaṃ kathaṃ cānyaṃ parijñāsyatyaśobhanam // 10.46 //
lāghavaṃ yāti lokasya dharmācca parihīyate /
nidhana puruṣairdṛṣṭaṃ madyajvalanasevanāt // 10.47 //
||madyapānaṃ kutsāṃ sampādayati
nāśo bhavatyatīte hi vartamāne suhṛjjane /
anāgate kutsitānāṃ madyaṃ traikālyanāśakam // 10.48 //
||madyaṃ dharmapradūṣakameva
nāmarūpavināśāya cittanāśāya dehinām /
utpannadoṣajanakaṃ madyaṃ dharmapradūṣakam // 10.49 //
||madyavarjanaṃ dharmāya pānañca mṛtyurna bhavati
samāhitā dharmaśīlāḥ puruṣā madyavarjakāḥ /
te yānti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra mṛtyurna vidyate // 10.50 //
// iti madyajugupsāvargo daśamaḥ //
||atha dvitīyam udānam
(cittañca vāk tathā karma saṃyojanantu pāpakam /
||narakapretatiryakkṣutkausīdyāni vidurdaśa // )
||(11) cittavargaḥ
||cittaṃ rājavat pravartate
agādhaṃ viṣamaṃ tīvraṃ sarvasattvagataṃ mahat /
cittaṃ sarvasya jagato rājavat sampravartate // 11.1 //
||cittadhāriṇastajjñāḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuvanti
adṛśyaṃ samprati bhayaṃ karma nārakacañcalāḥ /
ye cittadhāriṇastajjñāste gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim // 11.2 //
etannayati vyutthānametannayati durgatim /
tadevādyantamamalaṃ nirvāṇamadhigacchati // 11.3 //
manaḥ pūrvamaṅgamā dharmā manaḥ śreṣṭhā manomayāḥ /
manasā suprasannena bhāṣate vā karoti vā // 11.4 //
||cittavaśagasya cittamanudhāvati
yo na cittasya vaśagaścittaṃ tasyāntagaṃ sadā /
sa nirṇāśayati kleśān tamaḥ sūryodayo yathā // 11.5 //
||cittadagdhāḥ nāśaṃ yānti
cittaṃ śatruḥ paraṃ śatrurna śatruraparaḥ smṛtaḥ /
cittadagdhāḥ sadā sattvāḥ kāladagdhā yathā jaḍāḥ // 11.6 //
yaścittavaśamāpanno bālo mūḍho 'jitendriyaḥ /
tena duḥkhe samo nāsti nirvāṇaṃ tasya dūrataḥ // 11.7 //
||cittavaśagaḥ naraḥ narakamadhigacchati
āvarjyaḥ śatruraparo na cittāni (nigūhate) /
eṣa badhnāti puruṣo nṛpateryamaśāsane // 11.8 //
viṣayeṣu ratā nityaṃ na sa dharmaḥ kathañcana /
saddharmapathasammūḍho narakaṃ nayate mahat // 11.9 //
durdamānāṃ paraṃ cittamanīnāmagniruttamaḥ /
durdāntaṃ śīghragantṛ ca narakaṃ nayate dhruvam // 11.10 //
ye cittasya vaśaṃ yātā yātāste narakaṃ purā /
yaistu tad vāryate śīghraṃ na te duḥkhānugāminaḥ // 11.11 //
||cittānurūpaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhañca bhavati
yathā yathā (nṛṇāṃ) cittaṃ pariṇāmastathā tathā /
kalpānāṃ śubhakarttuśca pāpakarttuśca pāpakam // 11.12 //
cittāyattaṃ bhavet karma karmāyattaṃ mano bhavet /
cittakarma samutthāya saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ // 11.13 //
duṣṭena cetasā karma yaḥ karoti pumāniha /
pacyate narake tena jālinyā sa viḍambitaḥ // 11.14 //
||cittakarma evaṃ saṃsāraḥ
cittādhīnaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
cittapratyayajaṃ hyetat hetupratyayasambhavam // 11.15 //
cittena vañcitāḥ sattvā pāpasya vaśamāgatāḥ /
gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāt kāraṇāgramahābhayā(t) // 11.16 //
||na bhavet cittavaśago 'pi tu dharmavaśo bhavet
na gacchet cittavaśatāṃ gacched dharmavaśe sadā /
dharmacārī sukhī nityaṃ pāpacārī na śarmabhāk // 11.17 //
||cittāyattaṃ sarva phalam
cittāyattā kriyā sarvā cittāyattaṃ phalaṃ smṛtam /
vicittaṃ hi phalaṃ cittaṃ tathā phalamadhismṛtam // 11.18 //
cittena cintitaṃ sarva lokaścittabhavānugaḥ /
na hi tad vidyate sthānaṃ yanna cittavaśānugam // 11.19 //
||śubhasya nirvāṇasādhanatvam
mokṣa bandhanayormūlaṃ hetubhūtaṃ paraṃ matam /
śubhena mucyate janturaśubhenāśu badhyate // 11.20 //
||cittavaśagāḥ kadāpi nirvāṇaṃ nādhigacchanti
jālinyā mohitāḥ sattvāścittasya vaśamāgatāḥ /
nirvāṇaṃ nāpi gacchanti jātyandhā iva satpatham // 11.21 //
pañcendriyāṇi jitavān pāpaṃ bhuṅkte na karhicit /
ekacittaṃ tathā karma kurute vividhe bhave // 11.22 //
pañcaraṅgojjvalaṃ cittaṃ yathā dṛśyaṃ praśasyate /
pañcendriyavicitraṃ hi tathā karma bhave bhavet // 11.23 //
||cittakarttānekadhā bhavati
cittakartā hi puruṣo dṛśyairbhavati naikadhā /
cittaṃ cittakaraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvathā naiva dṛśyate // 11.24 //
||cittaṃ śobhanamaśobhanaṃ ca karma karoti
śobhanāśobhanaṃ citraṃ yathā bhittiḥ kṛtistathā /
śobhanāśobhanaṃ karma tathā cittaṃ karoti hi // 11.25 //
||cittānugaṃ karma
divārātrau yathā cittaṃ sthitaṃ bhavati citragam /
divārātrau tathā karma bhave samanuvartate // 11.26 //
akṛtvā sukṛtaṃ karma cittavṛttyanugā narāḥ /
patanti vivaśāḥ pāpe cittāriparivañcitāḥ // 11.27 //
karmacittakaro hyeṣa yatra yatra niyujyate /
caracittena mahatā taccittaṃ ca karotyayam // 11.28 //
pariṇāmaviśeṣeṇa yatra yatra niyokṣyate /
preṣyante tatra cittena tridhā tu gaticāriṇaḥ // 11.29 //
||cittasya damanaṃ sukhāvaham
cittādhināni vartante sarvakarmāṇi dehinām /
tasmāccittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ nayate padamacyutam // 11.30 //
durviṣahyasya laghunā yatra yatra nipātinaḥ /
cittasya damanaṃ sādhu cittaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvaham // 11.31 //
yena cittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ tena doṣāḥ sadā jitāḥ /
jitadoṣasya dhīrasya duḥkhaṃ naiva prapadyate // 11.32 //
||cittasya laghuceṣṭitameva duḥkham
yacca svakaṃ bhaved duḥkhaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ paratra ca /
tat sarvamaviṣahyasya cittasya laghuceṣṭitam // 11.33 //
||cittameva sarveṣāṃ prabhuḥ
sasurāsuranāgānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām /
prabhurekaḥ paraṃ cittaṃ rājā(hi)tribhavasya tat // 11.34 //
||cittabhrāntaduḥkhamaśnute
cittaṃ nayati deveṣu cittañca narabhūmiṣu /
cittaṃ nayatyapāye(ṣu) cittaṃ bhrāmayati prajāḥ // 11.35 //
cittād bhrāntasya naṣṭasya viṣayairmohitasya ca /
tṛṣṇayā dahyamānasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanuttamam // 11.36 //
||cittasya damanāt sukhānubhūtirbhavati
ekacāri sadāmūḍhaṃ durviṣahyaṃ mahābalam /
sampradāri sadādṛśyaṃ capalaṃ śīghragāminam // 11.37 //
evaṃ vidhaṃ hi ye cittaṃ damayanti manīṣiṇaḥ /
te mārabandhanātītāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam // 11.38 //
||capalaṃ cittaṃ narakāyopakalpyate
saṅkalpakuṭilaṃ tīvramagādhaṃ capalaṃ hi tat /
cittaṃ tamaḥśritaṃ śubhraṃ narakāyopakalpyate // 11.39 //
||doṣanirmukto 'cyutaṃ padaṃ prāpnoti
tadevaṃ doṣanirmuktaṃ nendriyārthavaśānugam /
aliptaṃ pāpakairdharmairnayate padamacyutam // 11.40 //
||śuddhaṃ cittaṃ śuddhe karmaṇi pravartate
hetupratyayajaṃ cittaṃ yogavāhi paraṃ ca tat /
pariṇāmavaśācchīghraṃ tathā tat sampravartate // 11.41 //
||cittānadhīnatve karma cañcalaṃ bhavati
ekaṃ karoti karmāṇi vividhāni calaṃ ca tat /
ekānekaṃ caraṃ sūkṣmaṃ kṣaṇādūrdhva na tiṣṭhati // 11.42 //
||saṃsārasya māyopamatvapratipādanam
durvijñeyaḥ sadā tasya niḥśarīrasya sarvadā /
ko 'sau nayati lokāntamatha kena ca gacchati // 11.43 //
gataśca tiṣṭhati kutra śarīrakarmakārakam /
dṛśyāni tasya karmāṇi sañcayo na ca dṛśyate // 11.44 //
damanaṃ duṣkaraṃ tasya yasya bhūtirna vidyate /
sarvasattvagataṃ ghoraṃ laghukāri ca cākṣuṣam // 11.45 //
pāpāt pāpataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ māyopamamidaṃ bhavet /
puṇyāt puṇyataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ samyagmārgasamāśritam // 11.46 //
||māyopamatvasamarthanam
na gatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva dṛśyate /
nīyate ca kṣataṃ sarva jātyuttarasamāni ca // 11.47 //
śastreṇa chidyate nedaṃ jvalanena ca dahayate /
chidyate dahyate caiva janaḥ sarvamacakṣuṣā // 11.48 //
dṛḍhaṃ yat karmarajjvādi naraṃ badhnāti duḥkhitam /
jātyantarasahastrāṇi nayate na ca dṛśyate // 11.49 //
||dāntameva cittaṃ sukhāvaham
muhūrtena śubhaṃ bhūtaṃ muhūrtenāśubhaṃ ca tat /
śubhāśubhābhyāṃ racitaṃ(cittaṃ) dāntaṃ sukhāvaham // 11.50 //
ṣaḍ bhirdvāraiḥ prasūteṣu viṣayeṣvatilolupam /
cittaṃ nayati lokāntaṃ vyasanaṃ na ca budhyate // 11.51 //
||viprasannacittasya śreyaskaratve 'nuttamaṃ sukhaṃ bhavati
viprasannaṃ yathā toyaṃ viprasannaṃ yathā nabhaḥ /
viprasannaṃ tathā cittaṃ nīyate sukhamuttamam // 11.52 //
janāḥ sātiśayā (dṛṣṭā) vitarkaviṣayodbhavāt /
pauravāścittarājñaste bhavanti sahacāriṇaḥ // 11.53 //
||cañcalaṃ manaḥ saṃsāre gatiṃ kārayati
dhāvati yatra ca manastatra dhāvantyajñāninaḥ /
parasparabalānnī (tā) bhramanti tribhavārṇa(va)m // 11.54 //
||viśeṣacittenottamā gatirbhavati
cittavaiśadya bhāvānāṃ viśeṣaḥ karmaṇāstathā /
na karmaguṇahīnasya viśeṣa upalabhyate // 11.55 //
||susamāhitacittasya praśaṃsā
susamāhitacittaḥ sa nityaṃ dharmānudarśakaḥ /
na doṣavaśamāyāti yathā divyastamonudaḥ // 11.56 //
||gṛhasthasya samyagdṛṣṭitve nirvāṇaprāptirbhavati
samyagdṛṣṭeścādhimātrā yasya cetasi vartate /
gṛhastho 'pi sa me jñeyo muktaḥ saṃsārabandhanāt // 11.57 //
||vijñā devalokaṃ gacchanti
kalyāṇanirmalaṃ yacca tato doṣeṇa bādhyate /
vijño (na) malamāpnoti devaloke sa jāyate // 11.58 //
||vinītacittāḥ sukhagāmino bhavanti
viṣayadvāracapalaṃ nadīkuṭilagāminam /
yairvinītamidaṃ cittaṃ te surāḥ śubhabhāginaḥ // 11.59 //
||adharmamārgaḥ kalyāṇāya na bhavati
adharmapathamāśritya janāḥ pāpavaśānugāḥ /
ciraṃ bhramanti saṃsāre cittena parikheditāḥ // 11.60 //
||cittaṃ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe parivartate
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe cittamidaṃ naikaśaḥ parivartate /
laghusvabhāvacapalaṃ māyāgandharvasannibham // 11.61 //
||cañcalacitto baddho bhavati
tasya bandhanameveṣṭaṃ jñānavijñānasammatam /
dūravṛttirmahāvegaḥ paridhāvatyanekadhā // 11.62 //
||dhṛtyā cittadhāriṇaḥ sukhamaśnute
hriyamāṇaṃ sadā cittamindriyārthe durāsadam /
sandhārayati yo dhṛtyā sa dhīraḥ pāragāmikaḥ // 11.63 //
dhṛtimajñānamohaṃ ca viṣayottānamānasam /
sandhārayati yo dhīmān sa loke paṇḍito naraḥ // 11.64 //
||śubhacittaṃ kāmāvarodhakaṃ bhavati
yo yathā kurute cittaṃ tathā kāmān sa paśyati /
śubhena kāmaśamanaṃ nāśubhena pravardhanam // 11.65 //
||apraśāntamatirduḥkhamāpnoti
śāntacittaṃmanāḥ kāmānasyatīha viṣāstravat /
apraśāntamatiḥ sarpamaṇivat tān sa paśyati // 11.66 //
||cittavaśago na śubhāṃ gatimāpnoti
indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca cittādhīnā bhavantyamī /
citta saṃśleṣayogena pariṇāmaḥ pravartate // 11.67 //
||dhīrapraśaṃsā
tasyaiva vyavadhānena dhīraśca pratibudhyate /
rūpasāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ pariṇāmaḥ kathaṃ pṛthak // 11.68 //
||cittasvarūpanirūpaṇam
yathā rūpaṃ tathā sarva viṣayāścittahetavaḥ /
cittaṃ dāntaṃ sadā śāntaṃ doṣamiśravigarhitam // 11.69 //
ekamekaṃ yathā śāli gandharūpe pṛthagvidhe /
saṃśleṣo yāti nānātvaṃ tathācittaṃ pravartate // 11.70 //
kriyāṃ hi tatra kurute yatra (cittaṃ) pradhāvati /
cittasaṃvāhanaṃ tadvākyaṃ loko 'yaṃ sampravartate // 11.71 //
viṣayād bhrāntamanasaś(cā)tivego mahābalaḥ /
cittaṃ(śānta)karaṃ dāntaṃ śivaṃ bhavati dehinām // 11.72 //
||dāntena cetasā tattvadarśanaṃ bhavati
tenādāntena śīghreṇa sarvapāpavihāriṇā /
bhrāmyate tribhavaḥ sarvaḥ na ca tattvaṃ sa paśyati // 11.73 //
||samīraṇaraṇodbhrānto lokaḥ saṃsāre bhramati
samīraṇaraṇodbhrānto yathā bhramati sāgaraḥ /
citteśvarasamāyukto loko 'yaṃ bhrāmyate sadā // 11.74 //
||cittaṃ śubhaṃ sukhamedhīta
śubhopanītaṃ cittaṃ(hi) śubheṣvevāpanīyate /
tathā śubhānucaritamaśnute teṣu dhāvati // 11.75 //
||yogavāhicittaṃ pratyayaṃ labhate
yogavāhi nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ vāyvambusamameva ca /
pratyayaśca yathā labhyastathā tat paridhāvati // 11.76 //
||cittaṃ pradhāvati parivartate ca
śīghraṃ pradhāvate cittaṃ śīghrañca parivartate /
śīghraṃ nayati deveśa (bhuvane) dāyabhūmiṣu // 11.77 //
||cittasya karttṛtvam
karttṛtvaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ bharttṛtvaṃ sarvakarmaṇām /
netṛtvaṃ sarvakarmāṇāṃ cittatvamiti lakṣyate // 11.78 //
||cittaṃ na viśvaset
na viśvaseddhi cittasya nityaṃ chidraprahāriṇaḥ /
durlabhasyāpi vaśyasya capalasya viśeṣataḥ // 11.79 //
||cittagativarṇanam
muhūrtena śubhaṃ yāti muhūrtena tathāśubham /
bhavatyavyākṛtaṃ śīghraṃ gatirasya na vidyate // 11.80 //
nāyatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva vidyate /
abhūtaḥ sambhavastasya bhūtvā ca pratigacchati // 11.81 //
||rūparahitaṃ cittam
nākāro vidyate tasya sañcayo 'pi na vidyate /
grahaṇaṃ tasya naivāsti niḥśarīrasya sarvataḥ // 11.82 //
||pratyayasādhanavarṇanam
hetupratyayasāmagrayā prāptaḥ sañjāyate punaḥ /
maṇisomapratyayo (hi) pratyayo jñāyate 'nalaḥ // 11.83 //
||cittamindriyarūpādīn prati dhāvati
tathaivendriyarūpādīn prativijñānasambhavaḥ /
naikasya jñāyate cittaṃ samavāyyanulakṣyate // 11.84 //
||cittaṃ durnivāryam
tadevaṃ viṣayaṃ matvā durnivārya ca sarvataḥ /
saddharmamatirāstheyā na kāmeṣu kathañcana // 11.85 //
||cittamati capalam
caṇḍāticapalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahāvalam /
cittaṃ karoti karmāṇi yanna paśyanti bāliśāḥ // 11.86 //
||duḥkhapravartakaṃ cittam
sarvasya karmaṇaścittaṃ hetubhūtaṃ bhave bhave /
bhavet pravartakaṃ duḥkhaṃ yena dhāvati bāliśaḥ // 11.87 //
||cittadoṣo mahādoṣa eva
vātādayo na doṣāḥ syurdoṣā rāgādayo matāḥ /
vātādibhirapāyeṣu mānavo nopapadyate // 11.88 //
cittadoṣo mahādoṣo nityaṃ(pāpa) vidarśakaḥ /
tasmātteṣāṃ samāśreyo na vātādigamādiha // 11.89 //
||rāgānugaṃ cittaṃ duṣṭaṃ bhavati
vātādayaḥ praṇaśyanti dehanāśāccharīriṇām /
(rāgādayo) na tasya syurjanmāntaraśatairapi // 11.90 //
tasmād rāgasya vaśagaṃ na vidheyaṃ kadācana /
ābhyantikaṃ paraṃ śreyaḥ prāpyate rāgasaṅkramāt // 11.91 //
||mana eva cikitsako bhavati
yaścittavaidyaḥ sa bhiṣag na śarīrabhiṣag bhṛśam /
manaścikitsako jñeyo na tathā laukiko mataḥ // 11.92 //
||svacittakarmaṇā dagdho narake patati
karmacintyaṃ samaṃ cintyaṃ na cittena prapadyate /
svacittakarmaṇā dagdho narakānupadhāvati // 11.93 //
||dhyānādeva cittaṃ śuddhaṃ bhavati
yacchreyaḥ samacittasya na tat (kvāpyupa)padyate /
saṃrakṣyaṃ hṛdayaṃ mūḍhaḥ prayātamanudhāvati // 11.94 //
||cittavaśago duḥkhamāpnoti
dhyānād dhyeyena kūṭena yaḥ pumān vanamāśritaḥ /
taṃ muktvā cittakaḥ so 'yaṃ saṃprahṛṣyati bāliśaḥ // 11.95 //
ye bālāścittapāśena cittakarmavicāriṇaḥ /
nīyante hyavaśā ghoraṃ narakaṃ karmamohitā // 11.96 //
||cittavaividhyanirūpaṇam
sucittamapi yaccitaṃ na taccittaṃ satāṃ matam /
karmacittaṃ mahācittaṃ tridhātugatacitritam // 11.97 //
sattvā citrairupāyairhi bhramanti gatipañcake /
tat sarva karmasācivyaṃ citrakartṛ vicitritam // 11.98 //
||cittavaśago baddho bhavati
cittacitrakareṇedaṃ karmajātaṃ vicitritam /
yena sarvamidaṃ baddhaṃ jagad bhramati mohitam // 11.99 //
varṣātaparajodhūmaiścittaṃ naśyati bhūbhujaiḥ /
kalpakoṭisahastreṇa citraṃ cittaṃ vinaśyati // 11.100 //
nāśaṃ prayāti basudhā sāgaraścāpi śuṣyati /
cittenāpi kṛtaṃ citraṃ tasyānubhavane sthite // 11.101 //
||pramatte citte nānāgatirbhavati
nānāgatisamāvṛttā nānākarmasamānugāḥ /
nānācittavaśāḥ sattvā bhramanti gatipañcake // 11.102 //
bāliśā (nāṃ)nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ viṣayaṃ(prati)dhāvati /
na cinotyaśubhaṃ karma yena dhāvati durgatim // 11.103 //
||cañcalaṃ cittaṃ sadā viṣamaṃ bhavati
tasmāccittaṃ sadā rakṣyaṃ cañcalaṃ viṣamaṃ kharam /
nityaṃ viṣayasaṃsaktaṃ tṛṣṇāviṣasamāvṛttam // 11.104 //
||viṣayānuraktaṃ cittaṃ vyasane pātayati
dhāvate viṣayaṃ caitad vyasanaṃ nāvabudhyate /
paścāttu vyasane prāpte phalaṃ vindati karmaṇaḥ // 11.105 //
||samāhitacittaḥ sukhamaśnute
apāyabhīrutā tasya tasya cittaṃ samāhitam /
samāhitena cittena sukhāt sukhamavāpnute // 11.106 //
||nirjitacittaḥ sukhamāpnoti
viṣamaṃ capalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahābalam /
yaiścittaṃ nirjitaṃ dhīraiste loke sukhino matāḥ // 11.107 //
// iti cittavarga ekādaśaḥ //
||(12) vāgvargaḥ
||nirvāṇābhilāṣukaḥ pāruṣyaṃ varjayet
pāruṣyaṃ varjayet dhīmān samyagvāg bhīrato bhavet /
mādhuryābhirato jarntunirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ // 12.1 //
vācaṃ paśyan sadābhāṣenmalināṃ ca vivarjayet /
vāṅmanenābhibhūtā ye te yānti narakaṃ narāḥ // 12.2 //
ekadharmavyatītasya mṛṣāvādasya dehinaḥ /
pratīrṇapratilokasya nākārya pāpamastiha // 12.3 //
||mṛṣāvāg na prayoktavyā
mṛṣāvācaṃ na bhāṣeta sarvā pratyayakārikām /
yathā badhyati saṃsāre sugatiṃ naiva paśyati // 12.4 //
sādhupratyayatenīhā sarvavidveṣakārikā /
kāntāraḥ sarvādharmāṇāṃ mṛṣāvāca pravartate // 12.5 //
jātamātrasya martyasya kaṭhārī jāyate mukhe /
paścāt chinattyātmānaṃ vācā durbhāṣitaṃ vadan // 12.6 //
sarvā kāryapatākā sā sarvapāpaprasūtikā /
tamasāṃ yonirekā sā yāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā // 12.7 //
satyena hīnāḥ puruṣāḥ sarvasādhuvivarjitāḥ /
tṛṇavad yānti loke 'smin pratyapāyeṣu duḥkhitāḥ // 12.8 //
na vadedanṛtaṃ dhīraḥ kaṣṭā hyanṛtavāditā /
pūtigandhyasukhī cāpi paścāttāpena tapyate // 12.9 //
||satyamahimā
satyaṃ ca na vivarjeta tasya dharmo na vidyate /
vinivartitadharmasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanekajam // 12.10 //
||satyaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ pradīpabhūtam
pradīpaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ ratnavat priyam /
svargasya ca paraṃ vartma satyamuktaṃ gatajvaraiḥ // 12.11 //
satyaṃ na hi divaṃ yāti mokṣasyāsatyavādinaḥ /
satyahīnā hi puruṣāḥ paśutulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // 12.12 //
jaghanyānāṃ jaghānyāste yeṣāṃ na vidyate /
satyaṃ dharmasya sopānaṃ jyotiṣāmākaro mahān // 12.13 //
panthāśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ dhanānāṃ dhanamuttamam /
pāpakaiśca (pari)trāṇāṃ satyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ // 12.14 //
||satyabhūṣitaṃ vāg bhūṣaṇasyāpi bhūṣaṇam
jyotiṣāṃ paramaṃ jyotiścakṣuścakṣuṣmatāmapi /
draviṇena vinā satyaṃ bhūṣaṇasyāpi bhūṣaṇam // 12.15 //
nidhānamatulaṃ satyamahārya (sarvasādhakam) /
gacchanti (satyā yiṇaḥ) puruṣāḥ paramāṃ gatim // 12.16 //
na tathā bhāsate rājā nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ /
satyena bhūṣito dhīmān śobhate devavad yathā // 12.17 //
na mātā na pitā cātha mitrāṇi na ca bāndhavāḥ /
trāṇamevaṃ yathā śrutvā tasmāt satyaparo bhavet // 12.18 //
||anṛtanindā
vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirviṣāṇāṃ paramaṃ viṣam /
durgatīnāṃ ca sopānamanṛtaṃ parikīrtitam // 12.19 //
viṣāgnitulyasaṃsparśa vartayedanṛtaṃ pumān /
anṛtena hi yo deva dagdhaityabhidhīyate // 12.20 //
||satyāsatyayoḥ parasparavirodhitvam
tasmāt sarvābhisāreṇa (na vadeda) nṛtaṃ pumān /
sarva bhayādikaṃ kaṣṭamanṛtaṃ kīrtitaṃ budhaiḥ // 12.21 //
vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirnirdahedapi sāgaram /
kiṃ punaryo mṛṣāvādī kāṣṭhaloṣṭhasamākṛtiḥ // 12.22 //
satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvādaṃ yo naraḥ pratipadyate /
ratnaṃ tyaktvā sa pāpātmā pāṣāṇaṃ pratipadyate // 12.23 //
yasyātmā na bhavet dviṣṭo yasya vā narakaṃ priyam /
mṛṣāvādaṃ svadehāgnim abuddhiḥ sa niṣevate // 12.24 //
sadedaṃ satyavacanaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvadehinām /
satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvāde kasmād yānti kubuddhayaḥ // 12.25 //
satyaṃ guṇānāmagryaṃ vai doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ smṛtam /
guṇāṃstyaktvā kathaṃ mūḍho doṣeṣu paridhāvati // 12.26 //
bījaṃ sarvasya duḥkhasya mṛṣāvādaḥ prakīrtitaḥ /
tathā satyaṃ sukhasyaiva tasmānnānṛtako bhavet // 12.27 //
satyavādī hi puruṣaḥ priyaḥ sarvasya dehinaḥ /
cakṣurdoṣaimṛṣāvādī tasmānnānṛtako bhavet // 12.28 //
devakalpāḥ sadā kṛṣṭāḥ puruṣāḥ satyavādinaḥ /
nārakeyāstathā mūḍhā janā hyanṛtacetasaḥ // 12.29 //
kalyāṇānāṃ paraṃ satyaṃ doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ tathā /
doṣavarjī guṇadveṣī puruṣaḥ puruṣottamaḥ // 12.30 //
sukhodayaṃ sukhodarkaṃ sukhena paripacyate /
sukhena labhate satyaṃ(satyaṃ) nirvāṇagāmikam // 12.31 //
duḥkhodayaṃ kaṭuphalaṃ duḥkhena saha pacyate /
anṛtaṃ sarvaduḥkhāntaṃ kaḥ pumān na vivarjayet // 12.32 //
nānyadeśāgataṃ satyaṃ nānyasmāt prārthyate hi tat /
sarvatīrthottamaṃ satyaṃ na tīrthasalilāvṛtam // 12.33 //
dīpānāṃ ca paro dīpaḥ satyaṃ buddhena deśitam /
auṣadhānāṃ paraṃ tacca sadā duḥkhaniṣūdanam // 12.34 //
amṛtañca viṣañcaiva jihvāpāśe sthitaṃ nṛṇām /
amṛtaṃ satyamityuktaṃ viṣaṃ tūktaṃ mṛṣāvacaḥ // 12.35 //
yasyānṛtamabhipretaṃ tasya satyaṃ dhruvaṃ sthitam /
viṣantu yasyābhimataṃ tasyeṣṭaṃ syānmṛṣāvacaḥ // 12.36 //
viṣeṇa niścitaṃ nāśo mṛṣāvādena niścitaḥ /
mṛtavat sa pumānasti yo mithyātvabhibhāṣate // 12.37 //
nātmano hi hitaṃ pathyaṃ (para)sya na kathañcana /
paścāttu paraduḥkhāya tat kathaṃ sevyate nṛbhiḥ // 12.38 //
deśe deśe mayā dṛṣṭaṃ janmamṛtyusahasrakam /
paraḥ sahastraṃ janayennāśayedanṛtaṃ vacaḥ // 12.39 //
abhijātasa niṣkarṣo dvijātīnāṃ ca bhūṣaṇam /
darśanaṃ mokṣamārgasya satyamityabhidhīyate // 12.40 //
tṛṣṇānadī hayamārāṇāṃ satāṃ satyena karmaṇām /
pūrvavat satyamityuktaṃ paraṃ sugatadeśikam // 12.41 //
anādinidhane loke tṛṣṇāpāraṅgatā (narāḥ) /
nāstyatrāṇaṃ yathā satyamiti dharmavido viduḥ // 12.42 //
||abhidhyāpāśo na sevanīyaḥ
satyavadhyā sadā kleśā vajravadhyā yathā nagāḥ /
hatā(ste) puruṣā (jñeyā ye ') bhidhyā parivañcitāḥ // 12.43 //
paracittasamenedaṃ rūpādyaiḥ parivañcyate /
abhidhyāmānasaṃ pāśaṃ sevitaṃ na vicakṣaṇaiḥ // 12.44 //
dahyate 'vikṛta ātmā tailadīptirivānalaḥ /
abhidhyādagdhamanasaḥ kāraṇaṃ nopalabhyate // 12.45 //
||vyāpādaḥ sattvān mohayatyeva
yasmāt tat sarvadā varjyaṃ kaṭukāśāviṣodayam /
vyāpādamohitāḥ sattvā nityaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ // 12.46 //
na śāntimadhigacchanti sarpā iva bileśayāḥ /
atha kūrasvabhāvā ye vyāpādaparamā narāḥ // 12.47 //
na teṣāṃ vidyate saukhyamādityena yathā tamaḥ /
na dharme nārthanikaro na dharmā na ca bāndhavāḥ // 12.48 //
rakṣanti puruṣān sarvān vyāpādāhatacetasaḥ /
tamasāmākaro hyeṣa vyāpāda iha kathyate // 12.49 //
vyāpādayati janakaṃ vyāpādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
avyāpādaḥ paraṃ śreyo na vyāpādaḥ kathañcana // 12.50 //
avyāpādaparā ye tu te yānti padamacyutam /
niyatātathavādī yo 'dharmavādī na dhārmikaḥ // 12.51 //
sa cauraḥ sarvalokasya na cauraḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ /
dharmavādī naro yastu carate dharmameva yaḥ // 12.52 //
sa yāti śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocyate /
mithyāvacohata (pumān) laukikaḥ samprakīrtyate // 12.53 //
lokottaraiḥ kalpaśataiḥ kadācit kathyate na vā /
tasmāt lokottaraṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ na kathañcana // 12.54 //
saṃsārabandhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ laukikaṃ viṣavad vacaḥ /
tṛṣṇārataḥ sadā puṇyānmucyateti suniścitam // 12.55 //
lokottaro (naro) dhanyo vidvadbhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ /
hitaṃ tattvaṃ ca yo mūḍho na gṛhṇāti gurorvacaḥ // 12.56 //
||satyavādī sadā devatābhiḥ puraskṛtaḥ
sa paścād vyasane prāpte tapyate svena cetasā /
satyavādī sadā dānto devatābhiḥ puraskṛtaḥ // 12.57 //
priyo bhavati lokasya paścād deveṣu modati /
priyo bhavati lokasya paścād svāntena(vardhate) /
darśanīyaṃ mukhaṃ cāsya devalokeṣu jāyate // 12.58 //
abhūtavādī puruṣaḥ sarvasattvopapātakaḥ /
tamonicayasaṅkāśo jīvannapi mṛtaḥ samaḥ // 12.59 //
kathaṃ na jihvā patitā vākyasaṃstutikattṛkā /
mṛṣā vadati yo vācaṃ sadbhūtaguṇanāśikām // 12.60 //
mukhe sannihito byālo mukhe sannihito 'phalaḥ /
(mukhe)sañjvalito vahniryo vācā bhāṣate mṛṣā // 12.61 //
jihvā saṅgrathitaiḥ pāśaiḥ narakasyāgrahetukaiḥ /
chettā ca dharmahetūnāṃ mṛṣāvādaḥ pravartate // 12.62 //
na tasya mātā na pitā buddho nāpi samvaraḥ /
yaḥ pāpabuddhiḥ patito mṛṣāvādaṃ prabhāṣateḥ // 12.63 //
akasmāllaghutāṃ yāti ṣaḍbhiśca parivartate /
mucyate devatābhiśca yo vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā // 12.64 //
asaṅgṛhītavākyasyāvicārya krodhanasya ca /
capalasyālpabhāgyasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanantakam // 12.65 //
parasya duḥkhaṃ dṛṣṭvāpi sattvaḥ sattvopapātakaḥ /
paravyasanavat tajjñaḥ pumān narakagāmikaḥ // 12.66 //
ye yathāvādino marttyā na ca tatkāriṇaḥ sadā // 12.67 //
||satyameva svargasya nirvāṇasya ca sopānam
satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ nirvāṇadvārameva tat /
tasmāt satyaparo nityaṃ nityaṃ dharmagatiḥ smṛtiḥ // 12.68 //
||anṛtaṃ na vadet
aśokamajaraṃ sthānaṃ prayāti puruṣottamaḥ /
varjayedanṛtaṃ dhīmān ninditaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ // 12.69 //
// iti vāgvargo dvādaśaḥ //
||(13) karmavargaḥ
||śubhāśubhakarmaṇāṃ phalabhogaḥ
śubhānāmaśubhānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ phalaniścayaḥ /
bhujyate sukṛtaṃ sarva karmabaddhā hi dehinaḥ // 13.1 //
(yadaṅgī)kriyate karma tatkṛdbhiranubhūyate /
cittamānena mūḍhena tṛṣṇānagaravāsinā // 13.2 //
||svayameva phalaṃ bhuṅkte
sahāyairbahubhiḥ sārdha kurute karma duṣkṛtam /
ekākī karmaṇastasya phalaṃ bhuṅkte bhave bhave // 13.3 //
karmaṇāmavisaṃyogaḥ sarvaiḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ /
śubhāśubhaṃ paraṃ loke gacchantamanugacchati // 13.4 //
yatra prayānti puṇyāni gandhastatrānudhāvati /
tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma gacchantamanugacchati /
svakarmaphaladāyādā prāṇena karmayojinaḥ // 13.5 //
||sukṛtaiḥ suralokaṃ gacchanti
sukṛtaiḥ suralokeṣu duṣkṛtaiśca tathāpyadhaḥ /
yadduḥkhaṃ karmaphalajaṃ jāyate kaṭukodayam // 13.6 //
tasyopamānamasuraṃ triṣu dhātuṣu jāyate /
tridoṣajaṃ tricittotthaṃ triṣu dhātuṣu pacyate // 13.7 //
tasya karmavipākasya triṣu dhātuṣu lakṣyate /
hetupratyayasāmagrīsamutthaṃ ca prameva tat // 13.8 //
||anyakṛtakarmaṇaḥ phalaṃ nānyo bhuṅkte
na hyanyena kṛtaṃ pāpamanyena paripacyate /
sukarmaphaladāyādaḥ prāṇināṃ sarva eva hi // 13.9 //
||pūrvoktānāṃ trividhānāṃ svasya kṛta eva vipāko bhavati
karmaṇastrividhasyāsya na cāpyanyasya pacyate /
catvāriṃśadvipākasya ghoraṃ bhavati ceṣṭitam // 13.10 //
||karmaphalavarṇanam
ekaḥ karoti karmāṇi ekaśca phalamaśnute /
ekastarati durgāṇi sahāyo jāyate 'paraḥ // 13.11 //
jalāpekṣī jano yastu kurute karma duṣkṛtam /
na jano janaśatānāṃ bhuṅkte hi vyañjanaṃ (kvacit) // 13.12 //
na hyanyena kṛtaṃ karma saṅkrāmatyaparasya tat /
na manye 'nādinidhanamasmiṃlloke na cāparaiḥ // 13.13 //
duḥkhāsvādaṃ sukhodbhūtaṃ yena duścaritaṃ kṛtam /
tena carati saṃsāre prerite karmavāyunā // 13.14 //
||kasya dharmo vardhate?
anapekṣitatattvasya vyākulīkṛtacetasaḥ /
vardhate sakalo (dharmaḥ) dharmāvṛtamanoharaḥ // 13.15 //
||ke narakaṃ gacchanti?
manasā vañcitāḥ sattvā manasā vipramohitāḥ /
gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāstamastamaparāyaṇāḥ // 13.16 //
tamovṛte hi saṃsāre durlabhaṃ buddhaśāsanam /
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti yebhyaḥ dharmo na rocate // 13.17 //
anādimati saṃsāre karmajālāvṛtā prajā /
jāyate bhriyate cai(va) svakarmaphalahetunā // 13.18 //
jāyante narake devā nārakeyāstathāvidhāḥ /
manuṣyāḥ pretaviṣaye narakaṃ vā prayānti hi // 13.19 //
||sukarmaṇaiva sukham
anyonyaprabhavaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vā sukham /
kleśadharmodbhave janmanyaparādikṛtaṃ ca tat // 13.20 //
asaṅkhyeyakṛtaṃ karma saṃsāre prāṇibhiḥ sadā /
tatra śakyaṃ budhairgantuṃ varjayitvā tathāgataiḥ // 13.21 //
nādharmasya phalaṃ sādhu viparītaṃ na pacyate /
hetoḥ sadṛśatā dṛṣṭā jalasya vividhasya vai // 13.22 //
sādṛśyasya hetuphalaṃ viparītaṃ na jātu hi /
saṃskṛtānāmarūpāṇāṃ hetuḥ pratyayasambhavaḥ // 13.23 //
||sahetukaṃ sarva karmaphalam
nāhetukaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narake tu viśeṣataḥ /
hetusaṅghātasaṃsaktaṃ narakeṣu vipacyate // 13.24 //
kṛtoparatagāḍhānāṃ niyataṃ pāpagāminām /
karmaṇā phalasambandho narakeṣu vipacyate // 13.25 //
deśānāṃ prati kālaṃ tu yat karma (vi)nivartate /
tasya neṣṭaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tattvamārgavidarśakaiḥ // 13.26 //
||udāharaṇapradarśanapūrvakaṃ phalasya karmādhīnatvameveti
dīpādhīnā prabhā yadvat karmādhīnaṃ phalaṃ tathā /
anyo 'nyaphalasambhūtaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sarva eva hi // 13.27 //
||pratītyasamutpādasamarthanam
anyonyahetukā dṛṣṭā hyanyonyavaśavartinaḥ /
sādṛśyasyānubandhena dṛśyante tattvadarśakaiḥ // 13.28 //
nāhetuphalasandhānamīśvarādibhirāsthitam /
bhavanti saṃskṛtā dharmā deśitāstattvadarśibhiḥ // 13.29 //
anādimatisaṃsāre hetupratyayasambhave /
sādṛśyaṃ karmaṇā dṛṣṭaṃ viparītaṃ na kalpyate // 13.30 //
||buddhasya svarūpam
tatstheṣu karmavaśagāḥ prāṇinaḥ karmahetujāḥ /
sa karmaphalatattvajño (buddha) ityabhidhīyate // 13.31 //
||keṣāṃ śāntiḥ na vidyate?
mārgāmārgaviruddhā ye mūḍhā buddhasya śāsane /
(na) teṣāṃ vidyate śāntirādityasya tamo yathā // 13.32 //
||karmāyattaṃ sukham
karmāyattaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sukhāyattaṃ manastathā /
mano 'vaboddhayā(ste)dharmā ye vyutpattivicāriṇaḥ // 13.33 //
||sucaritasya karmaṇaḥ phalam
anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārā jalabud budasannibhāḥ /
tasmāt sucaritaṃ karma loke martya paratra ca // 13.34 //
dṛṣṭaṃ karmaphalaṃ loke dṛṣṭā eva vicitratā /
yaḥ pramādaparaḥ puṃsāstasyātmā dhruvamapriyaḥ // 13.35 //
karmarajjvātidṛḍhayā duṣpramokṣasugāḍhayā /
baddhā bālā na gacchanti nirvāṇapuramuttamam // 13.36 //
// iti karmavargastrayodaśaḥ //
||(14) saṃyojanavargaḥ
||jñānena nirvāṇādhigamaḥ
jñānaśastre(ṇa)tāṃ chitvā nirmuktā vigatajvarā /
prayānti nirvṛttiṃ dhanyā yatra jñānyeva vidyate // 14.1 //
sadṛśaṃ hi phalaṃ hetoḥ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ /
hetorasadṛśaṃ naiva phalaṃ pacati dehinām // 14.2 //
hetupratyayasambaddhajanmapratyayasaṅgatāḥ /
yathā baddhā hi saṃsāre pramucyante (na)dehinaḥ // 14.3 //
||paramaśānterūpāyaḥ
tāṃ viśliṣya susambaddhāṃ gāḍhāṃ durviṣehāṃ parām /
gacchanti paramāṃ śānti yatra duḥkhaṃ na vidyate // 14.4 //
karmaṇā niyataṃ jantuḥ karmaṇā paripacyate /
sūpagaṃ (nanu) saṃsāre sukhaṃ naivopalabhyate // 14.5 //
duḥkhe duḥkhābhiṣaktānāṃ jantūnāṃ mūḍhacetasām /
sanmārgadeśiko nāsti yo 'smād duḥkhāt pramocayet // 14.6 //
ye na dharmaparā nityaṃ ye na satyaparāḥ sadā /
ye ca yoniratā nityaṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na hīyate // 14.7 //
||dharma iha paratra ca sukhāvahaḥ
mātṛvat pitṛvaccaiva (mitravad) bandhuvat sadā /
dharmo vai deśito buddhairiha loke paratra ca // 14.8 //
trigatyavasthitāḥ sattvāstridoṣavaśamāgatāḥ /
tridhātugatikā nityaṃ trilokyāṃ patitāḥ (janāḥ) // 14.9 //
trikarmopāntavaśagāḥ strīpānādiparāśca ye /
na bhavānmuktigatikāḥ syurbhūmau vicaranti te // 14.10 //
||keṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate?
triratne (na) pramādyanti tribodhivaśagāśca ye /
tridṛṣṭivarjakā ye tu teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate // 14.11 //
trikālasthitisaṃlagnā vijvarāstattvadarśinaḥ /
tribhāgakṛtisantuṣṭā vītaśokā nivṛttigāḥ // 14.12 //
trirāśisamavetā ye trikarmapravicāriṇaḥ /
na te vatsyanti saṃsāre vītadoṣā gatajvarāḥ // 14.13 //
mārgāmārgavidhijñā ye bhāvābhāvavicintakāḥ /
maitrībhāvaviviktā ye te yānti paramāṃ gatim // 14.14 //
||naraḥ kān bhajet?
anāvilena(manasā) viprasannena (cetasā) /
sarvadā dharmavaśagān dhīrān viprān bhajennaraḥ // 14.15 //
satyameva prapannā ye smṛtyā (hitvā) manomalam /
bhāvābhilāṣād viratā muktā niḥsaṃśayaṃ hi te // 14.16 //
nityaṃ duḥkhasukhairbaddhā vipralabdhā hyanekaśaḥ /
narā nidhanatāṃ yānti prāṇino mohavañcitāḥ // 14.17 //
||kairdurguṇaiḥ svargo na labhyate?
nāhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ kausīdyaṃ pāpamitratā /
naitāni nākabījāni tebhyo rajyenna paṇḍitaḥ // 14.18 //
āhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ nityaṃ pāpānucāriṇaḥ /
naraḥ prapātāt patati sa paścāt pratibudhyate // 14.19 //
||krodherṣyādibhayagrastāḥ svarga na gacchanti
krodherṣyāstyānamiddhaṃ hi tvaśraddhaṃ yanmanastathā /
mohaśokabhayagrastā na svarga prabhavanti te // 14.20 //
amṛtaṃ madyapānaṃ ca mithyādṛṣṭiśca lubdhatā /
kāraṇāni karaṇasya vyāpādakrūrakarmatā // 14.21 //
||kudṛṣṭeḥ kuphalam
adarśanaṃ paraṃ śreyo na kudṛṣṭiḥ kathañcana /
kudarśanena saṃmūḍhāḥ prayānti narakaṃ narāḥ // 14.22 //
ahetuṃ hetumāpaśyantya (nityaṃ) nityavannarāḥ /
prayānti narakaṃ tīvraṃ mithyāvādena vañcitāḥ // 14.23 //
kaṣṭena tejasā teṣāṃ mithyādarśanatatparāḥ /
prajñābhimānino bhūtā mohayantyaparān janān // 14.24 //
mohāndhakāragahane patantyeva mahārṇave /
loke prakṛtiduḥkhe 'smin hetubhūtā hi te janāḥ // 14.25 //
śarāṇāṃ tāpanaṃ kṣepaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ /
cittatā yā tudatyante sarvataḥ kleśaparvataḥ // 14.26 //
kleśanāgād vimokṣo yo yasya jñānapuraḥ saraḥ /
prāpyate vītakai rūpaiḥ puruṣaistattvadarśibhiḥ // 14.27 //
anyo 'nyamatibhiḥ sarvā loko 'yaṃ vipralobhitaḥ /
na yāti paramāṃ śāntiṃ yatra mithyā na kathyate // 14.28 //
||narakahetavaḥ
auddhatyapāpasaṃsargaḥ kausīdyaṃ lubdhatā tathā /
hetavo narakasyaite śīlasya hi vivarjanam // 14.29 //
madyapānaṃ sadā hiṃsā paradārābhidarśanam /
lobhaḥ kūrā matiścaiva hetavo narakasya te // 14.30 //
||nāśahetavaḥ
paiśunyaṃ pāpasaṃsargo mithyādṛṣṭirasaṃyamaḥ /
cāpalyaṃ manasaścaiva nāśayanti naraṃ sadā // 14.31 //
avidyayā saha pāruṣyaiḥ mithyāvāgabhimānitā /
na sukhāya bhavantyete asmiṃlloke na cāpare // 14.32 //
||ke parivarjanīyāḥ?
yadyasau bhramati prāyo lokesmin kinna cāpare /
yadyasambhrāmite loke ye ca duḥkhe nimajjati // 14.33 //
tacceṣṭitamavidyāyāḥ kathayanti tathāgatāḥ /
mithyāmāno 'timānī ca sarvathā (parivarjyatām) /
parivarjyāḥ sadā hyete duḥkhavṛkṣasya hetavaḥ // 14.34 //
jñāninaḥ paramodārā nityaṃ kleśavadhe ratāḥ /
chitvā (tad) bandhanaṃ sarva gacchanti padamacyutam /
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇamasmiṃlloke na cāpare // 14.35 //
||doṣasevanaiḥ nāśo bhavati
doṣāṇāṃ sevanaṃ dṛṣṭamavidyāsampravartakam /
varjanīyāḥ sadā kleśāḥ sevyaṃ jñānamanuttamam // 14.36 //
||jñānena muktirbhavati
jñānena muktirbhavati na ca kleśairihocyate /
jñānāgninā hi dahayante kleśakāṣṭhā na śeṣataḥ // 14.37 //
||kāmamayajñānaṃ kleśajanakam
kleśaiḥ kimartha saṃruddhā jālinī viṣa(yai) ratā /
punaḥ kāmamayaṃ jñānaṃ cakṣuḥpaṭalabādhakam // 14.38 //
||rāganindā
nirvāṇayati sambuddhavākyabhaiṣajyabhojanaiḥ /
saddharmasenāpatinā rāgasenā vigarhitāḥ // 14.39 //
||śubhā vāṇī prayoktavyā
udīritā śubhā vāṇī niścetavyā prayatnataḥ /
catvāro hi viparyāsā budbudavaccakāsate /
lokadharmāstathā cāṣṭau nāśayantyakhilaṃ jagat // 14.40 //
||jñānaplavaḥ santaraṇasamarthaḥ
jālinīprabhavā nadyo vitarkaśatadustarāḥ /
jñānaplavaṃ samāruhya taranti munayaḥ śivāḥ // 14.41 //
||keṣāṃ muktirna vidyate?
mūḍhā ye bhūtamanaso narāḥ kāmasya sevinaḥ /
sadā ca pañcabhiḥ sthānairmuktisteṣāṃ na vidyate // 14.42 //
ayoniśomanaskārairyo vahniḥ samudīryate /
sa yoniśomanaskāravarṣaṇaiḥ pratikalpate // 14.43 //
||avidyāsaṃbhavam andhatvaṃ kathaṃ dūrībhavet?
andhatvaṃ cirakālotthamavidyāsambhavaṃ nṛṇām /
tadalpakāle jātena pradīpena na paśyati // 14.44 //
||jñānalokena trayo doṣāḥ vinaśyanti
rāgamūḍhā vipacyante narake mandamedhasaḥ /
jñāninastu na naśyanti nirvāṇagamanā yathā /
trayo do(ṣā) vinaśyanti jñānalokena dehinām // 14.45 //
tasmādaśeṣavijñānaśīlakṣāntirato bhavet /
amūḍhānāṃ praṇaśyanti trayo doṣāḥ śarīriṇām // 14.46 //
jñānānalena mandaśca kleśendhana mahāttviṣaḥ /
vyādhinirmagnatanavaḥ śayyāveṣṭanagocarāḥ // 14.47 //
yatra yāti paraṃ vedaṃ manomohamayaṃ phalam /
yāni duḥkhānyanekānyanekā bhujyate gatiḥ // 14.48 //
pañcakaiḥ prāṇibhinityametanmohasya ceṣṭitam /
trayo vā nirjitā doṣā yairidaṃ dahyate jagat // 14.49 //
||jñānayogena sukhaṃ bhavati
tamagniṃ jñānayogena nirvāpya sukhito bhavet /
tasmājjñānāgninā nityaṃ nirdahet kleśaparvatam /
kleśaparvatadagdhasya sukhaṃ padamavasthitam // 14.50 //
// iti saṃyojanavargaścaturdaśaḥ //
||(15) pāpavargaḥ
||pāpaphalasya ajñātā paritāpaṃ labhate
kriyamāṇasya pāpasya vijñeyaṃ kaṭukaṃ phalam /
yo na jānāti mūḍhātmā paścāt sa paritapyate // 15.1 //
(phalaṃ ca) labhate puruṣaḥ sarvapāpasya karmaṇaḥ /
tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ // 15.2 //
alpādapi mahāghorāt narakāt pāpacetasaḥ /
muktyartha (tāni) pāpāni bhūyo mohavaśaṃ gatāḥ // 15.3 //
na viśvaseddhi pāpasyā(lpatāṃ) narakagāmikām /
alpena vahninā śaile dahayante sarvato drumāḥ // 15.4 //
||nāsti pāpasamo śatruḥ
pāpena narakaṃ yāti pāpena paridahyate /
pāpena naiti nirvāṇaṃ nāsti pāpasamo ripuḥ // 15.5 //
pāpācāro hi puruṣo na kvacit sukhamedhate /
(pāpaṃ) tasmānna seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ // 15.6 //
sādhukāraṃ ca sādhūnāṃ pāpamārgasya duṣkaram /
kurvantaḥ pāpakān sattvā modante(laghucetasaḥ) // 15.7 //
vipākakaṭukaḥ paścāt paritāpo 'lpacetasaḥ /
kuto 'pacitagātrasya karmaṇo dṛśyate phalam // 15.8 //
tasmāt pāpaṃ na kurvīta kaṣṭā pāpasya vedanā /
pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca pāpināṃ pacyate dhruvam // 15.9 //
na hi pāpaṃ na pāpasya tasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet /
parivarjitapāpasya na pāpād bhayamasti hi // 15.10 //
svakṛtaṃ bādhate pāpaṃ parīkṣyaṃ naiva bhujyate /
kalyāṇasya phalaṃ sādhu kaṣṭaṃ pāpasya pacyate // 15.11 //
kṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ pāpaṃ kalyāṇaṃ nānusevate /
na śastrāgniprapātebhyo duḥkhaṃ syāt tādṛśaṃ nṛṇām // 15.12 //
yathā niṣevitaṃ mithyāpāpaṃ pāpeṣu kalpyate /
vinivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ // 15.13 //
||śāntasya bhikṣornirvāṇaṃ nātidūram
(dehino) śāntavaktrasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ /
tīvrāt tīvrataraṃ yānti narāḥ kukṛtakāriṇaḥ // 15.14 //
sukhāt sukhataraṃ yānti narāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ /
na hi tīvrasya pāpasya sukhaṃ phalamavāpyate // 15.15 //
sukhasya vā phala tīvraṃ viparītaṃ na pacyate /
anādimati saṃsāre sukṛtānāṃ phalaṃ sukham // 15.16 //
karmaṇāṃ sukṛtānāṃ ca tathā duḥkhaphalaṃ smṛtam /
pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śubhasya ca śubhaṃ tathā // 15.17 //
||pāpī narakeṣupapadyate
pāpācāraḥ śubhadveṣī narakeṣūpapadyate /
parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ // 15.18 //
hastāvalambi nirvāṇamadṛṣṭaṃ tadanāvilam /
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇā dharmā nityaṃ sukhodayāḥ // 15.19 //
||tasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet
ādimadhyāntakaṭukaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ /
tasmāt pāpaṃ sadā varjyamālambyañca śubhaṃ sadā // 15.20 //
parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ sukhamavasthitam /
anādimati saṃsāre dagdhāḥ pāpaiḥ punarnarāḥ /
khedaṃ kasmānna gacchanti bālā mohavaśānugāḥ // 15.21 //
āpātamadhuraṃ pāpaṃ pariṇāme 'gnisannibham /
pāpakārī tu puruṣaḥ sarvaloke vigarhitaḥ /
śubhakārī sadā śāntastasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet // 15.22 //
||dhīraistattvanidarśakaiḥ pāpavivarjanam
aniṣṭamahitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vipāke kaṭuvedanam /
pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca tasmād dhīmān vivarjayet // 15.23 //
asti pāpaṃ dhruvaṃ pāpe pāpamasti na pātakam /
pāpāceṣṭā kṣayāpekṣā kṛpā cittasugāmitā // 15.24 //
pāpaṃ pāpāśritaṃ nityaṃ dharmo dharmāśritastathā /
unnayatyuktametaddhi dhīraistattvanidarśakaiḥ // 15.25 //
||pāpavirahitāḥ paramaṃ sukhaṃ prāpnuvanti
acetanā dhruvaṃ bālā yeṣāṃ duścaritaṃ priyam /
vinivarjitapāpāstu gacchanti paramāṃ gatim // 15.26 //
atīva vañcanāghorā niyatā pāpagāminī /
mānuṣyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya yasya pāpaṃ priyaṃ bahu // 15.27 //
||śubhāśubhaphalayoḥ pariṇāmabhedaḥ
pāpād virajyate yastu śubhe vātīva rajyate /
sa sukhāt sukhamāpnoti nivṛttiṃ vā prayāti hi // 15.28 //
naro bhavati dhanyo 'yaṃ yaḥ śubhānyupasevate /
sa tvadhanyatamo loke yaḥ pāpamupasevate // 15.29 //
ādimadhyāntanidhanaṃ sadbhireva vigarhitam /
pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narakāyopakalpyate // 15.30 //
||śubhakarmā sukhamāpnoti devalokaṃ ca gacchati
atīva śobhate loke śubhakarmā jitendriyaḥ /
kāyasya bhedāt satataṃ devaloke sa jāyate // 15.31 //
||pāpasya pariṇāmaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
||duṣkṛtasyānubaddhaṃ hi duṣkṛtaṃ phalamucyate
sukṛtasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ sukhavipākajam /
bījasyāśuvibhītasya pariṇāmaḥ sudāruṇaḥ // 15.32 //
nimittaṃ sadṛśaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ /
pāpenākṛṣyate jantuḥ durgatau baḍiśairiva // 15.33 //
baḍiśairmucyate mīnaḥ pāpaṃ pāpānna mucyate /
dina pīḍāpi pāpasya sarvathā duḥkhakārikā // 15.34 //
amedhyasya yathā gandhaḥ pratikūlo hi dehinām /
śubhasya vāsanā ramyā vipraṇaṣṭasya durgatau // 15.35 //
vileṣu vāsanaṃ yadvat puṣpe naṣṭe pradṛśyate /
calatyayaṃ pāpakārī nityaṃ kāmavaśānugaḥ // 15.36 //
||ke śubhacāriṇaḥ?
ālasyānṛtiko nityaṃ nāsau kalyāṇamarhati /
anantā rajanī teṣāṃ (yeṣāṃ) pāpe sthitaṃ manaḥ // 15.37 //
prabhātaṃ rajanī teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ pāpe sthirā matiḥ /
anīrṣyakāḥ sakalyāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ śubhacāriṇaḥ // 15.38 //
||alpapāpī sukhamāpnute
ye na pāpātmano bhūtāste nityaṃ koṭacāriṇaḥ /
alpabhārā yathā nāvā plavate na nimajjati // 15.39 //
||pāpīmitreṇa duḥkhaṃ bhavati
tathālpapāpapuruṣaḥ plavate na nimajjati /
na pāpamitrasaṃsargāt puruṣaḥ sukhavān bhavet // 15.40 //
pāpamitraṃ samāsādya sarvānalaparo bhavet /
karmārambha vidhijño yo nityaṃ sūkṣmārtha (darśakaḥ) // 15.41 //
nāsau limpati pāpena paṅkena gaganaṃ yathā /
aśrutaṃ puruṣaḥ śṛṇvan śrutañcāpi bhaved dṛḍham // 15.42 //
||paṇḍitalakṣaṇam
pāpaṃ ca varjayed dhīmān pretya deveṣu jāyate /
guṇadoṣaparijñānammetat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam // 15.43 //
||mūḍhalakṣaṇam
guṇadoṣāparijñānametanmūḍhasya lakṣaṇam /
guṇeṣu guṇasañcāro doṣeṣu ca tathaiva ca // 15.44 //
||mūḍhāmūḍhayorlakṣaṇam
sadoṣaguṇatattvajño nityaṃ bhavati śokabhāk /
pāpakarttā (tu) puruṣaḥ śatruvaccātmanaḥ sthitaḥ // 15.45 //
śubhakarttā tathā puṃso mitravat pratipadyate /
tamonirayabhūmiṣvamṛto 'yaṃ pratipadyate // 15.46 //
yasya pāparatā buddhirnityaṃ viṣayatatparā /
viṣayārāmacapalā nityaṃ rāgānucāriṇī // 15.47 //
yasya buddhirna dharmeṣu narasya duḥkhabhāginaḥ /
hetutaśca mahāduḥkhāntahetorvahnisaṃyutāt // 15.48 //
kṣīṇapāpā vayaṃ sarve bhūyo lokamihāgatāḥ /
sukṛtasya phalaṃ sādhu hyanekaguṇamaṇḍitam // 15.49 //
duṣkṛtasya phalaṃ duḥkhaṃ visaṃvādakamiṣyate /
te vayaṃ sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ bhūyāma bhavasaṅkaṭe // 15.50 //
karmavāyusamudbhrāntāḥ samudrasya yathormayaḥ /
kṛtaṃ pāpeṣvamanasaḥ pāpaiḥ rakṣanti ye janāḥ // 15.51 //
te tasya hetornarakaṃ prayāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ /
tasmāttu narakānmuktāḥ te gacchanti triviṣṭapam // 15.52 //
te hi duḥkhaṃ (na)saṃsmṛtya punaḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ /
kharībhūtamidaṃ cittaṃ dolādolaiḥ sukhāsukhaiḥ // 15.53 //
viyogo 'yaṃ parīghāto na ca duḥkhairna vidyate /
apāradārasaṃyukta indriyaiḥ parivañcitaḥ // 15.54 //
||tṛṣṇāpāśavaśagaḥ saṃsāre bhramati
jano bhramati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāpāśavaśānugaḥ /
narakāt pretabhuvanaṃ tiryagyoniṣu pretataḥ // 15.55 //
tiryagbhyo nākabhuvanaṃ nākād bhūyo nṛjātiṣu /
ekakarmaparibhrānto jagad bhramati cakravat // 15.56 //
||sarva duḥkham
na ca khedavaśaṃ yānti(hyabhyāsa) vaśamāgatāḥ /
rakṣanti nākabhuvanaṃ virajyante tathā sukhaiḥ // 15.57 //
sukhāt sukhaparibhrāntā bhramanti bhramacāriṇaḥ /
duḥkhaṃ padmasahasrāṇi padmakoṭiśatāni ca // 15.58 //
(tāni) duḥkhāni bhuṅktāni na ca kliśyanti bāliśāḥ /
na sukhaṃ vidyate loke sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pariplutam // 15.59 //
||duḥkhasya hetuḥ bhavati
udvegaṃ naiva gacchanti prāṇino mohapīḍitāḥ /
duḥkhena khidyate bālo duḥkhahetau ca vartate // 15.60 //
hetau śataphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bījaṃ prati yathā phalaiḥ /
sukhaduḥkhakaśābaddhāḥ prāṇinastribhavānugāḥ // 15.61 //
na yānti paramaṃ kṣemaṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitam /
smaryate (hi) yadā duḥkhaṃ tadā vidhyati dehinam // 15.62 //
vismṛte ca punarduḥkhe caranti vigatajvarāḥ /
nārakaṃ tu sadā duḥkhaṃ smṛtaṃ bhavati dehibhiḥ // 15.63 //
tadā kṛṣṇamidaṃ saukhyamanumānena tiṣṭhati /
tadeva viditaṃ matvā jagat sarva samanvitam // 15.64 //
śreyasi kriyatāṃ buddhirdoṣebhyo vinivāryate /
kṣaṇādhikāracapalaṃ jīvitaṃ veti vartate // 15.65 //
kṣīyante cāpi karmāṇi tasmācchreyaḥparo bhavet /
cittavegaṃ manaḥ sarva jīvitaṃ veti vartate // 15.66 //
||anāgatād duḥkhāt jñānī na bibheti
tasmānna jīvikāhetau pāpaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ /
anāgatasya duḥkhasya na vibheti mahājanaḥ // 15.67 //
yenā(sya) pacyate pāpaṃ mohapāpavaśaṅgatam /
mohitaḥ pāpakairdhamairaśubhaiḥ śuklavarjitaiḥ // 15.68 //
||mūḍhaḥ pāpavaśād narakaṃ gacchati
nīyate narakaṃ mūḍho yatra pāpaṃ vipacyate /
yasya pāpād bhayaṃ nāsti sa pāpaṃ kurute bahu // 15.69 //
sa pāpānantasandagdhaḥ paścānnarakamāpnute /
(api) sūkṣmāgnikaṇikā yathā dāhāya kalpate // 15.70 //
||pāpavirahitāḥ sukhamicchanti
anyairapi tathā pāpairnarakaṃ yāntyabuddhayaḥ /
apāpabhīrutā tasmāt kartavyā sukhamicchatā // 15.71 //
hiṃsā mithyāvaco 'brahmacarya bhūyaḥ sukhodayam /
āhrīkyamanapatrāpyamauddhatyaṃ pāpamitratā // 15.72 //
||viṣāgnisadṛśaṃ pāpam
viṣāgnisadṛśā hayete tebhyo rakṣet prayatnataḥ /
duḥkhaṃ hi māradharmo 'yaṃ sukhaṃ dharmasamantataḥ // 15.73 //
||sukhaduḥkhayorlakṣaṇam
lakṣaṇaṃ(sukha) duḥkhānāṃ vidustattvavido janāḥ /
satyaṃ dānaṃ tathā kṣāntiḥ sadā cāpāpamitratā /
maitrī sadābhibhūteṣu prasthānaṃ tridivasya (hi) // 15.74 //
// iti pāpavargaḥ pañcadaśaḥ //
||(16) narakavargaḥ
||aṣṭau narakāgnayaḥ
kṛtvā duṣkṛtakarmāṇi sattvā viṣamajīvinaḥ /
yā gatiḥ pretya gacchantī tānapāyān (hi me) śṛṇu // 16.1 //
sañjīvaṃ kāmasūtraṃ ca sampātaṃ dvau ca rauravau /
tamoparaṃ mahācitrapatanaṃ ca pratāpanam // 16.2 //
ityete narakā aṣṭāvākhyātā duratikramāḥ /
raudrakarmābhisaṅkīrṇāḥ pratyekaṃ kṣobhadā (matāḥ) // 16.3 //
||narakāgnīnāṃ bhayānakatvam
catuḥskandhāścaturdvārā vibhaktā bhāgaśo mitāḥ /
ayaḥ prākāraparyantā ayasā pratiduḥkhitāḥ // 16.4 //
taptāyomayasaṃ bhūmirjvalantī tejasodgatā /
anekayojanaśataṃ dahati svaciṃṣā(bhṛśam) // 16.5 //
kandarpadamanā ghorā arciṣmanto durāsadāḥ /
romaharṣaṇarūpāste 'pyāhurduḥkhā bhayānakāḥ // 16.6 //
||narake patitā bhṛśaṃ tapyante
ete patanti narake ūrdhvapādā avāṅmukhāḥ /
ṛṣīṇāmativaktāraḥ saṃyatānāṃ tapasvinām // 16.7 //
te punastatra pacyante taptāmbhasi kṛtā iva /
krandamānā divārātrau, nagā vāteritā iva // 16.8 //
praṇadanti mahānādaṃ tīvraduḥkhaiḥ pratāpitāḥ /
sarvā diśaśca dhāvanti nārakaiḥ puruṣairdrutāḥ // 16.9 //
kudṛṣṭyā mohayitvārthe mohapāśāvṛto janaḥ /
prāpnoti narakaṃ ghoraṃ kāraṇodadhisaṃvṛtaḥ // 16.10 //
kudṛṣṭyā dagdhasarvasvo manuṣyaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ /
tathā baddho 'sti narake mānināṃ ghorakāraṇam // 16.11 //
ye mithyāvaśamāpannāḥ puruṣā mandamedhasaḥ /
te sarve narakaṃ yānti cittairhi parivañcitāḥ // 16.12 //
||kukṛtaphalam
yastvayā duṣkṛtaṃ pūrva kṛtaṃ cittānuvartinā /
tasya bhuṅktaphalaṃ mūḍha vipākottama (māpsyasi) // 16.13 //
hāryāṇi paricittāni, saṃsevyāḥ parayoṣitaḥ /
hrasvā (hi) jantavo nityaṃ svacittaparivañcitāḥ // 16.14 //
tasya karmavipākasya vaśa eva tvamāgataḥ /
kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukarma puruṣādhama! // 16.15 //
ye narāḥ kukṛtaṃ kṛtvā pañcatvaṃ yāntyamedhasaḥ /
yeṣāṃ tu niṣphalaṃ janma bījamuptaṃ yathoṣare // 16.16 //
alpamādhuryasaṃyuktān kāmān kaṭuvipākinaḥ /
sevate yastvasau mūḍhaḥ sa yāti tamaso tamaḥ // 16.17 //
kiṃ kṛtaṃ mūḍha bhavatā putradārasukhārthinā /
dahasye narake caikaḥ svakarmaphalavañcitaḥ // 16.18 //
||keṣāṃ duṣkaraṃ jīvanam?
yaḥ putradāravaśagaḥ sevate duṣkaraṃ naraḥ /
sa yāti narakatvaṃ (ca) pāpaṃ tadanubhūyate // 16.19 //
na dārā na sutā nārtha na mitrāṇi kathañcana /
mṛtyukāle samutpanne rakṣanti samupasthitāḥ // 16.20 //
yeṣāṃ sāṃkleśikaṃ cittaṃ tṛṣṇayā parivañcitam /
sahāyatā kutasteṣāṃ kasmāt (tvaṃ) paritapyase? // 16.21 //
hṛto 'si pūrvaviṣayaistṛṣṇayā parivañcitaḥ /
kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukṛtaṃ mūḍhacetanaḥ // 16.22 //
na tathāgnirna śastrāṇi na viṣaṃ nārayaḥ sthitāḥ /
bādhate puruṣaṃ loke yathā duṣkṛtyamātmajam // 16.23 //
||pakṣiṇāṃ nīḍavāsavat bhavacakram
digbhāge hi yathā gatvā saṃśrayante vanaspatīn /
vihagāḥ kālamutthāya tathā prāṇisamāgamaḥ // 16.24 //
nāśayitvā paraṃ dravyaṃ kṛtvā lokavyatikramaṃ /
kiṃ karotyaśubhaṃ karma mohena parivañcitaḥ // 16.25 //
yena yāti parāṃ śāntiṃ yena yātyasurālayam /
tatra hetuḥ paraṃ mohastamasāmapi yat tamaḥ // 16.26 //
||kuṭumbāya kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ narake pātayati
putradāramayaiḥ pāśaiścānītā narakālayam /
yadartha kriyate pāpaṃ yuṣmābhiścittavañcitaiḥ // 16.27 //
mitrāṇi putrāḥ (pitarau kiṃ) bandhujanabāndhavāḥ /
yeṣāmarthe kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhavadbhirmandabuddhibhiḥ // 16.28 //
nūnamātmā na te kānto babhūva narabhūmiṣu /
yena tvayā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ putrārthena narādhamaḥ // 16.29 //
yena pūrvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paścānna paritapyate /
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ putrakāraṇavañcitaḥ // 16.30 //
